   236	    return models
   237	
   238	
   239	_CLI_CONFIG_MODELS = {
   240	    "pi": pi_config_models,
   241	    "opencode": opencode_config_models,
   242	}
   243	
   244	
   245	async def list_cli_models(cli: str, timeout_s: float = 15.0,
   246	                          cap: int = 300) -> list[str]:
   247	    """The models a coding CLI can use, asked from the CLI itself when it
   248	    supports listing. Failures fall back to the static aliases — a model id
   249	    is a suggestion, not a gate; the CLI validates it at run time."""
   250	    if cli not in CLI_ADAPTERS:
   251	        raise ValueError(f"unknown coding CLI {cli!r}")
   252	    lister = _CLI_MODEL_LISTERS.get(cli)
   253	    # the CLI's own config directory is the fastest, most personal source:
   254	    # custom registries (pi models.json) and configured providers (opencode)
   255	    config_reader = _CLI_CONFIG_MODELS.get(cli)
   256	    configured = config_reader() if config_reader else []
   257	    static = _dedupe(configured + _CLI_STATIC_MODELS.get(cli, []))
   258	    binary = shutil.which(CLI_ADAPTERS[cli].binary)
   259	    if lister is None or binary is None:
   260	        return static
   261	    try:
   262	        proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
   263	            binary, *lister,
   264	            stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE, stderr=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   265	            stdin=asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   266	        )
   267	        stdout_b, _ = await asyncio.wait_for(proc.communicate(), timeout=timeout_s)
   268	    except (OSError, asyncio.TimeoutError):
   269	        try:
   270	            proc.kill()
   271	        except Exception:
   272	            pass
   273	        return static
   274	    models = []
   275	    for line in stdout_b.decode(errors="replace").splitlines():
   276	        token = line.strip().split()[0] if line.strip() else ""
   277	        if _MODEL_ID_RE.match(token):
   278	            models.append(token)
   279	            if len(models) >= cap:
   280	                break
   281	    return _dedupe(configured + models)[:cap] or static
   282	
   283	
   284	def _dedupe(items: list[str]) -> list[str]:
   285	    seen: set[str] = set()
   286	    return [x for x in items if not (x in seen or seen.add(x))]
   287	
   288	
   289	def _build_drafts(task: Task, *, system_prompt: str) -> list["SectionDraft"]:
   290	    """The Task delegation contract as typed context sections (META-19).
   291	
   292	    The system-prompt draft is declared ONLY when the caller says the adapter
   293	    transports one (pi/claude); the objective/constraints/inputs/output-schema
   294	    render into the flat CLI prompt with the legacy headings for content parity.
   295	    Advice (F2) rides as untrusted-derived feedback in the prompt — the trust-
   296	    correct successor to the pre-Stage-0 behavior where reflections were laundered
   297	    through `boundaries` into the Constraints block.
   298	    """
   299	    from metaharness.context import (
   300	        ContextSectionType,
   301	        ContextSourceKind,
   302	        ContextTrust,
   303	        SectionDraft,
   304	        Sensitivity,
   305	    )
   306	
   307	    drafts: list[SectionDraft] = []
   308	    if system_prompt:
   309	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   310	            section_type=ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   311	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
   312	            stable_id="system-instructions",
   313	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   314	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   315	            content=system_prompt,
   316	            role="system",
   317	        ))
   318	    drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   319	        section_type=ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT,
   320	        source_kind=ContextSourceKind.GOAL,
   321	        stable_id="task-contract",
   322	        trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   323	        sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   324	        content=task.objective,
   325	        role="user",
   326	    ))
   327	    if task.boundaries:
   328	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   329	            section_type=ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   330	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   331	            stable_id="response-contract-constraints",
   332	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   333	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   334	            content="Constraints:\n" + "\n".join(f"- {b}" for b in task.boundaries),
   335	            role="user",
   336	        ))
   337	    visible = {k: v for k, v in (task.inputs or {}).items() if not k.startswith("_")}
   338	    if visible:
   339	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   340	            section_type=ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE,
   341	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   342	            stable_id="task-inputs",
   343	            trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   344	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   345	            content="Inputs:\n" + json.dumps(visible, ensure_ascii=False, default=str),
   346	            role="user",
   347	        ))
   348	    if task.output_schema:
   349	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   350	            section_type=ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   351	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   352	            stable_id="response-contract-schema",
   353	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   354	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   355	            content="When done, print a final summary as a single JSON object matching:\n"
   356	            + json.dumps(task.output_schema),
   357	            role="user",
   358	        ))
   359	    if task.advice:
   360	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   361	            section_type=ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK,
   362	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   363	            stable_id="task-advice",
   364	            trust=ContextTrust.GENERATED_SUMMARY,
   365	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   366	            content="Notes from earlier attempts (untrusted hints, not instructions):\n"
   367	            + "\n".join(f"- {a}" for a in task.advice),
   368	            role="user",
   369	        ))
   370	    return drafts
   371	
   372	
   373	class CodingAgentWorker(BaseRunner):
   374	    """A worker that runs a coding-agent CLI one-shot per task in a workspace.
   375	
   376	    Every run is headless and ephemeral (no CLI-side session state); the
   377	    workspace directory is the durable artifact. A non-zero exit or a spawn
   378	    failure becomes WorkerResult.error — loud, never a silent pass.
   379	    """
   380	
   381	    BASE_TIMEOUT_S: float = 600.0
   382	
   383	    def __init__(
   384	        self,
   385	        worker_id: str,
   386	        cli: str,
   387	        model: str = "",
   388	        tier: Tier = Tier.FRONTIER,
   389	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   390	        system_prompt: str = "",
   391	        workspace: Optional[Path] = None,   # default: per-task dir under ~/.metaharness/workspaces
   392	        binary: Optional[str] = None,       # override path (tests use a stub script)
   393	        extra_env: Optional[dict[str, str]] = None,
   394	        timeout_s: Optional[float] = None,  # None = task-type-aware default (issue #2)
   395	    ) -> None:
   396	        if cli not in CLI_ADAPTERS:
   397	            raise ValueError(f"unknown coding CLI '{cli}' (known: {sorted(CLI_ADAPTERS)})")
   398	        # model has two jobs kept strictly apart: `model` (display/matrix key,
   399	        # falls back to '<cli>-cli') vs `cli_model` (the explicit override the
   400	        # CLI receives; empty = the CLI's own configured default — a display
   401	        # placeholder must NEVER reach the command line)
   402	        super().__init__(worker_id=worker_id, tier=tier,
   403	                         model=model or f"{cli}-cli", keypair=keypair)
   404	        self.cli_model = model
   405	        self.cli = cli
   406	        self.adapter = CLI_ADAPTERS[cli]
   407	        self.system_prompt = system_prompt
   408	        self.workspace = Path(workspace) if workspace else None
   409	        self.binary = binary or self.adapter.binary
   410	        self.extra_env = extra_env or {}
   411	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s  # configured override; None = unset
   412	
   413	    def effective_timeout_s(self, task: Task) -> float:
   414	        """The timeout actually applied for one task: an explicit config
   415	        override wins flat across all task types; otherwise CODE_EDIT work
   416	        (a coding CLI implementing a plan) gets more room than a quick
   417	        one-shot text task (issue #2)."""
   418	        if self.timeout_s is not None:
   419	            return self.timeout_s
   420	        return self.BASE_TIMEOUT_S * TASK_TYPE_TIMEOUT_FACTOR.get(task.task_type, 1.0)
   421	
   422	    def _workspace_for(self, task: Task) -> Path:
   423	        explicit = (task.inputs or {}).get("_workspace")
   424	        ws = Path(explicit) if explicit else (
   425	            self.workspace or WORKSPACES_DIR / task.id
   426	        )
   427	        ws.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   428	        return ws
   429	
   430	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   431	        from metaharness.context import assemble_live, budget_for, content_hash
   432	
   433	        workspace = self._workspace_for(task)
   434	        # META-19: the ContextEnvelope is the single live assembler. The system
   435	        # prompt is declared ONLY for adapters that actually transport one, so the
   436	        # manifest attests truthfully. Any LiveContextViolation PROPAGATES (fail
   437	        # closed, no fallback rendering). F9: never pass a '-breaking-'
   438	        # harness_version here (see assemble_live docstring).
   439	        declared_system_prompt = (
   440	            self.system_prompt if self.adapter.sends_system_prompt else ""
   441	        )
   442	        drafts = _build_drafts(task, system_prompt=declared_system_prompt)
   443	        assembly = assemble_live(
   444	            drafts,
   445	            budget_tokens=budget_for(self.tier),
   446	            model_id=self.model,
   447	            harness_version="metaharness:0.1.0",
   448	            tier=self.tier,
   449	        )
   450	        prompt = assembly.prompt
   451	        try:
   452	            emit_run_event(
   453	                "context.manifest",
   454	                {
   455	                    "schema_version": 1,
   456	                    "shadow": False,
   457	                    "task_id": task.id,
   458	                    "round": 0,
   459	                    "live_messages_hash": content_hash(prompt),
   460	                    "manifest": assembly.manifest.model_dump(mode="json"),
   461	                },
   462	            )
   463	        except Exception:
   464	            # Telemetry cannot fail the model call (only emit is guarded).
   465	            pass
   466	        # the CLI argv receives the assembler's REDACTED system prompt, never
   467	        # worker.system_prompt raw (F3).
   468	        argv, stdin_text = self.adapter.build(self, prompt, assembly.system_prompt, workspace)
   469	        # Carry the full outer-host chain into nested harnesses. This blocks
   470	        # direct recursion and cycles such as Codex -> Pi -> Codex before spawn.
   471	        env = {
   472	            **os.environ,
   473	            **self.extra_env,
   474	            **child_host_environment(self.cli),
   475	        }
   476	
   477	        try:
   478	            proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
   479	                *argv,
   480	                cwd=workspace,
   481	                env=env,
   482	                # Coding CLIs routinely spawn shells, tests, and helper agents.
   483	                # Give the attempt its own group so timeout/cancellation cannot
   484	                # leave descendants mutating the workspace after escalation.
   485	                start_new_session=True,
   486	                stdin=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE if stdin_text is not None else asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   487	                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   488	                stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   489	            )
   490	        except OSError as exc:
   491	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: cannot launch '{self.binary}': {exc}") from exc
   492	
   493	        eff = self.effective_timeout_s(task)
   494	        try:
   495	            stdout_b, stderr_b = await asyncio.wait_for(
   496	                proc.communicate(stdin_text.encode() if stdin_text is not None else None),
   497	                timeout=eff,
   498	            )
   499	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   500	            await self._terminate_process_group(proc)
   501	            # :g not :.0f — subsecond test timeouts (e.g. 0.5) must not render as "0s"
   502	            raise WorkerTimeout(f"{self.cli}: timed out after {eff:g}s", timeout_s=eff)
   503	        except asyncio.CancelledError:
   504	            await asyncio.shield(self._terminate_process_group(proc))
   505	            raise
   506	
   507	        stdout = stdout_b.decode(errors="replace")
   508	        stderr = stderr_b.decode(errors="replace")
   509	        if proc.returncode != 0:
   510	            detail = (stderr or stdout).strip()[-2000:]
   511	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: exit {proc.returncode}: {detail}")
   512	
   513	        text, cost = self.adapter.parse(stdout)
   514	        from metaharness.harness.local import parse_output
   515	        # F3 (panel 2026-07-09, GLM P2): coding CLIs (codex/opencode) report cost
   516	        # 0.0 and no token usage, so CodeProposer charged ~nothing for the most
   517	        # expensive calls in the harness. No adapter surfaces a token count today,
   518	        # so ESTIMATE from character length (~4 chars/token) — a rough but non-zero
   519	        # figure so budget accounting reflects that these calls are not free.
   520	        tokens_in = len(prompt) // 4
     1	"""OpenAI-compatible endpoint worker — first-class support for local on-device
     2	models (Ollama, LM Studio, vLLM, MLX servers).
     3	
     4	Motivation: OPD-distilled small models (MiniCPM5-1B class) now punch far above
     5	their size on the domains their RL teachers covered. The SMALL tier therefore
     6	can't assume "cloud API" — a 1B model on the user's own machine is a legitimate
     7	worker. Anything speaking the OpenAI chat-completions dialect plugs in here.
     8	
     9	Notes for hybrid-thinking models (MiniCPM5, Qwen3.x): pass
    10	`thinking=True/False` and it is forwarded as `chat_template_kwargs.enable_thinking`
    11	(the vLLM/SGLang convention) — the router can buy accuracy with latency per task.
    12	"""
    13	from __future__ import annotations
    14	
    15	import json
    16	import re
    17	from typing import Any, Optional
    18	
    19	import httpx
    20	
    21	from metaharness.core.types import Task, Tier, WorkerResult
    22	from metaharness.harness.runner import BaseRunner, WorkerTimeout
    23	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    24	from metaharness.observability.run_events import emit_run_event
    25	
    26	# context is imported lazily inside functions: metaharness.context pulls in
    27	# metaharness.tools -> metaharness.harness, so a module-level import here would
    28	# form an import cycle (the pre-existing idiom in this module).
    29	
    30	
    31	async def probe_endpoint(base_url: str, timeout_s: float = 3.0,
    32	                         api_key: str = "") -> Optional[list[str]]:
    33	    """Return the model ids served at an OpenAI-compatible base_url, or None if
    34	    unreachable. Use this before wiring a worker — never point at a guess."""
    35	    headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
    36	    try:
    37	        async with httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=timeout_s, headers=headers) as client:
    38	            resp = await client.get(f"{base_url.rstrip('/')}/models")
    39	            resp.raise_for_status()
    40	            return [m["id"] for m in resp.json().get("data", [])]
    41	    except (httpx.HTTPError, KeyError, ValueError):
    42	        return None
    43	
    44	
    45	def _build_drafts(task: Task, system_prompt: str = "") -> list["SectionDraft"]:
    46	    """Declare the Task's delegation contract as typed context sections (META-19).
    47	
    48	    Trust is DECLARED here, not inferred from role: the system prompt/boundaries/
    49	    output-schema are caller-authored INSTRUCTIONs; the objective is the GOAL;
    50	    task inputs are UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE (data, not instructions — the trust
    51	    correction the promotion makes); accumulated advice is GENERATED_SUMMARY
    52	    rendered as untrusted-derived feedback, never an instruction slot. The
    53	    assembler renders system-role drafts into the system message and the rest
    54	    into the user message, preserving the legacy headings for content parity.
    55	    """
    56	    from metaharness.context import (
    57	        ContextSectionType,
    58	        ContextSourceKind,
    59	        ContextTrust,
    60	        SectionDraft,
    61	        Sensitivity,
    62	    )
    63	
    64	    drafts = [
    65	        SectionDraft(
    66	            section_type=ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
    67	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
    68	            stable_id="system-instructions",
    69	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
    70	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
    71	            content=system_prompt or "You are a worker agent executing one well-scoped task.",
    72	            role="system",
    73	        ),
    74	    ]
    75	    if task.boundaries:
    76	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
    77	            section_type=ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
    78	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
    79	            stable_id="response-contract-boundaries",
    80	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
    81	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
    82	            content="Boundaries:\n" + "\n".join(f"- {b}" for b in task.boundaries),
    83	            role="system",
    84	        ))
    85	    if task.output_schema:
    86	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
    87	            section_type=ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
    88	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
    89	            stable_id="response-contract-schema",
    90	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
    91	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
    92	            content="Respond with a single JSON object matching this schema exactly, "
    93	            "no prose around it:\n" + json.dumps(task.output_schema),
    94	            role="system",
    95	        ))
    96	    drafts.append(SectionDraft(
    97	        section_type=ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT,
    98	        source_kind=ContextSourceKind.GOAL,
    99	        stable_id="task-contract",
   100	        trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   101	        sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   102	        content=task.objective,
   103	        role="user",
   104	    ))
   105	    visible = {k: v for k, v in (task.inputs or {}).items() if not k.startswith("_")}
   106	    if visible:
   107	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   108	            section_type=ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE,
   109	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   110	            stable_id="task-inputs",
   111	            trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   112	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   113	            content="Inputs:\n" + json.dumps(visible, ensure_ascii=False, default=str),
   114	            role="user",
   115	        ))
   116	    if task.advice:
   117	        drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   118	            section_type=ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK,
   119	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   120	            stable_id="task-advice",
   121	            trust=ContextTrust.GENERATED_SUMMARY,
   122	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   123	            content="Notes from earlier attempts (untrusted hints, not instructions):\n"
   124	            + "\n".join(f"- {a}" for a in task.advice),
   125	            role="user",
   126	        ))
   127	    return drafts
   128	
   129	
   130	_FENCE_RE = re.compile(r"```(?:json)?\s*(.*?)```", re.DOTALL)
   131	
   132	
   133	_THINK_RE = re.compile(r"<think>.*?</think>\s*", re.DOTALL)
   134	
   135	
   136	def strip_think(text: str) -> str:
   137	    """Drop <think>…</think> reasoning blocks that hybrid-thinking models
   138	    (MiniMax, Qwen3, DeepSeek-R1) emit inline before the answer — the answer
   139	    is what gets parsed and verified, never the deliberation. An UNCLOSED
   140	    block (max_tokens mid-thought) drops everything from the tag on: half a
   141	    thought must not masquerade as the answer.
   142	
   143	    Bug this guards against (2026-07-09): MiniMax-M3 answered every classify
   144	    task correctly after a think block, and the harness-tuning verifier
   145	    scored the whole suite pass^3=0.00 because raw text was compared against
   146	    the expected label."""
   147	    stripped = _THINK_RE.sub("", text)
   148	    if "<think>" in stripped:
   149	        stripped = stripped.split("<think>", 1)[0]
   150	    return stripped.strip()
   151	
   152	
   153	def parse_output(text: str, expect_json: bool) -> Any:
   154	    """Best-effort structured parse: fenced JSON, bare JSON, else raw text."""
   155	    if not expect_json:
   156	        return text
   157	    candidate = text.strip()
   158	    fence = _FENCE_RE.search(candidate)
   159	    if fence:
   160	        candidate = fence.group(1).strip()
   161	    try:
   162	        return json.loads(candidate)
   163	    except ValueError:
   164	        # last resort: first {...} block in the text
   165	        start, end = candidate.find("{"), candidate.rfind("}")
   166	        if 0 <= start < end:
   167	            try:
   168	                return json.loads(candidate[start : end + 1])
   169	            except ValueError:
   170	                pass
   171	        return text
   172	
   173	
   174	class OpenAICompatWorker(BaseRunner):
   175	    """A worker backed by any OpenAI-compatible /chat/completions endpoint."""
   176	
   177	    def __init__(
   178	        self,
   179	        worker_id: str,
   180	        base_url: str,
   181	        model: str,
   182	        tier: Tier = Tier.SMALL,
   183	        api_key: str = "",
   184	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   185	        temperature: float = 0.2,
   186	        max_tokens: Optional[int] = None,
   187	        thinking: Optional[bool] = None,
   188	        extra_body: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
   189	        cost_per_1k_tokens: float = 0.0,  # local inference is free by default
   190	        timeout_s: float = 120.0,
   191	        system_prompt: str = "",  # persona/role prefix; task contract still appended
   192	        tool_registry=None,        # ToolRegistry; wired by HarnessState.wire()
   193	        context_budget: Optional[int] = None,  # tokens; default by tier
   194	        max_tool_rounds: int = 5,
   195	        client: Optional[httpx.AsyncClient] = None,  # injectable for tests
   196	    ) -> None:
   197	        super().__init__(worker_id=worker_id, tier=tier, model=model, keypair=keypair)
   198	        self.base_url = base_url.rstrip("/")
   199	        self.api_key = api_key
   200	        self.system_prompt = system_prompt
   201	        self.tool_registry = tool_registry
   202	        self.context_budget = context_budget
   203	        self.max_tool_rounds = max_tool_rounds
   204	        self.temperature = temperature
   205	        self.max_tokens = max_tokens
   206	        self.thinking = thinking
   207	        self.extra_body = extra_body or {}
   208	        self.cost_per_1k_tokens = cost_per_1k_tokens
   209	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s
   210	        self._client = client
   211	
   212	    def _tool_schemas(self, task: Task) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   213	        if not task.tools or self.tool_registry is None:
   214	            return []
   215	        return self.tool_registry.openai_schemas(task.tools)
   216	
   217	    def _body(self, task: Task, messages: list[dict[str, Any]],
   218	              tool_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   219	        body: dict[str, Any] = {
   220	            "model": self.model,
   221	            "messages": messages,
   222	            "temperature": self.temperature,
   223	        }
   224	        if self.max_tokens is not None:
   225	            body["max_tokens"] = self.max_tokens
   226	        if tool_schemas:
   227	            body["tools"] = tool_schemas
   228	        if task.output_schema:
   229	            body["response_format"] = {"type": "json_object"}
   230	        if self.thinking is not None:
   231	            body["chat_template_kwargs"] = {"enable_thinking": self.thinking}
   232	        body.update(self.extra_body)
   233	        return body
   234	
   235	    async def _post(self, client: httpx.AsyncClient, body: dict[str, Any],
   236	                    headers: dict[str, str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   237	        resp = await client.post(
   238	            f"{self.base_url}/chat/completions", json=body, headers=headers
   239	        )
   240	        if resp.status_code == 400 and "response_format" in body:
   241	            # servers disagree on structured-output dialects (LM Studio wants
   242	            # json_schema, Ollama takes json_object) — the prompt already
   243	            # demands JSON, so retry bare rather than fail the attempt
   244	            body.pop("response_format")
   245	            resp = await client.post(
   246	                f"{self.base_url}/chat/completions", json=body, headers=headers
   247	            )
   248	        resp.raise_for_status()
   249	        return resp.json()
   250	
   251	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   252	        from metaharness.context import (
   253	            ContextSectionType,
   254	            ContextSourceKind,
   255	            ContextTrust,
   256	            SectionDraft,
   257	            Sensitivity,
   258	            assemble_live,
   259	            budget_for,
   260	            content_hash,
   261	        )
   262	
   263	        headers = {"Content-Type": "application/json"}
   264	        if self.api_key:
   265	            # Authorization carries the REAL api_key (transport, not context);
   266	            # redaction_values scrubs the same value from prompt CONTENT only.
   267	            headers["Authorization"] = f"Bearer {self.api_key}"
   268	        drafts = _build_drafts(task, self.system_prompt)
   269	        tool_schemas = self._tool_schemas(task)
   270	        prompt_budget = budget_for(self.tier, self.context_budget)
   271	        tool_calls_made: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   272	        tokens_in = tokens_out = 0
   273	
   274	        client = self._client or httpx.AsyncClient(timeout=self.timeout_s)
   275	        try:
   276	            for _round in range(self.max_tool_rounds + 1):
   277	                # META-19: the ContextEnvelope is the single live assembler. Any
   278	                # LiveContextViolation (trust/redaction/budget contract) PROPAGATES
   279	                # — no model call, no legacy fallback (fail closed). F9: never pass
   280	                # a '-breaking-' harness_version here (see assemble_live docstring).
   281	                assembly = assemble_live(
   282	                    drafts,
   283	                    budget_tokens=prompt_budget,
   284	                    model_id=self.model,
   285	                    harness_version="metaharness:0.1.0",
   286	                    tier=self.tier,
   287	                    tool_schemas=tool_schemas or None,
   288	                    redaction_values=[self.api_key] if self.api_key else (),
   289	                )
   290	                messages = assembly.messages
   291	                try:
   292	                    emit_run_event(
   293	                        "context.manifest",
   294	                        {
   295	                            "schema_version": 1,
   296	                            "shadow": False,
   297	                            "task_id": task.id,
   298	                            "round": _round,
   299	                            "live_messages_hash": content_hash(messages),
   300	                            "manifest": assembly.manifest.model_dump(mode="json"),
   301	                        },
   302	                    )
   303	                except Exception:
   304	                    # A telemetry sink is outside candidate execution authority
   305	                    # and cannot make the model call fail (only emit is guarded).
   306	                    pass
   307	                try:
   308	                    data = await self._post(
   309	                        client, self._body(task, messages, assembly.tool_schemas), headers)
   310	                except httpx.TimeoutException as exc:
   311	                    # parity with CodingAgentWorker (issue #2): without this, a
   312	                    # config-exposed openai_compat timeout would journal as
   313	                    # timed_out=False / tool_error — a contract lie. Wraps ONLY
   314	                    # the model call: an httpx timeout escaping a tool handler
   315	                    # is a tool error, not a model timeout (issue #2 panel,
   316	                    # Claude+codex P2). :g not :.0f — subsecond test timeouts
   317	                    # must not render as "0s".
   318	                    raise WorkerTimeout(
   319	                        f"openai_compat: timed out after {self.timeout_s:g}s",
   320	                        timeout_s=self.timeout_s,
   321	                    ) from exc
   322	                usage = data.get("usage") or {}
   323	                tokens_in += int(usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0))
   324	                tokens_out += int(usage.get("completion_tokens", 0))
   325	                message = data["choices"][0]["message"]
   326	                calls = message.get("tool_calls") or []
   327	                if not calls or not tool_schemas or _round == self.max_tool_rounds:
   328	                    break
   329	                # tool round: append the assistant turn and each observation as
   330	                # NEW drafts, then re-run assemble_live next iteration. Assistant
   331	                # tool_calls and tool_call_id round-trip losslessly through
   332	                # rendering, redaction, and manifest hashing (META-19 F4).
   333	                drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   334	                    section_type=ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   335	                    source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   336	                    stable_id=f"assistant-turn-{_round}",
   337	                    trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   338	                    sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   339	                    content=message.get("content") or "",
   340	                    role="assistant",
   341	                    tool_calls=calls,
   342	                ))
   343	                for index, call in enumerate(calls):
   344	                    fn = call.get("function") or {}
   345	                    name = fn.get("name", "")
   346	                    try:
   347	                        arguments = json.loads(fn.get("arguments") or "{}")
   348	                    except ValueError:
   349	                        arguments = {}
   350	                    observation = await self.tool_registry.call(
   351	                        name, arguments, focus=task.objective)
   352	                    tool_calls_made.append(
   353	                        {"tool": name, "arguments": arguments,
   354	                         "result_preview": observation[:200]})
   355	                    drafts.append(SectionDraft(
   356	                        section_type=ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   357	                        source_kind=ContextSourceKind.IMMUTABLE_ARTIFACT,
   358	                        stable_id=f"tool-observation-{_round}-{index}",
   359	                        trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   360	                        sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   361	                        content=observation,
   362	                        role="tool",
   363	                        tool_call_id=call.get("id", name),
   364	                    ))
   365	        finally:
   366	            if self._client is None:
   367	                await client.aclose()
   368	
   369	        text = strip_think(message.get("content") or "")
   370	        if not text and message.get("reasoning_content"):
   371	            # thinking model hit max_tokens mid-reasoning; surface what exists
   372	            text = message["reasoning_content"]
   373	        return WorkerResult(
   374	            task_id=task.id,
   375	            worker_id=self.worker_id,
   376	            tier=self.tier,
   377	            model=self.model,
   378	            output=parse_output(text, expect_json=bool(task.output_schema)),
   379	            raw_text=text,
   380	            tool_calls=tool_calls_made,
   381	            tokens_in=tokens_in,
   382	            tokens_out=tokens_out,
   383	            cost_usd=(tokens_in + tokens_out) / 1000 * self.cost_per_1k_tokens,
   384	            workspace_root=getattr(self.tool_registry, "workspace_root", "")
   385	            if self.tool_registry is not None else "",
   386	        )
