   422	    def _workspace_for(self, task: Task) -> Path:
   423	        explicit = (task.inputs or {}).get("_workspace")
   424	        ws = Path(explicit) if explicit else (
   425	            self.workspace or WORKSPACES_DIR / task.id
   426	        )
   427	        ws.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   428	        return ws
   429	
   430	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   431	        from metaharness.context import assemble_live, budget_for, content_hash
   432	
   433	        workspace = self._workspace_for(task)
   434	        # META-19: the ContextEnvelope is the single live assembler. The system
   435	        # prompt is declared ONLY for adapters that actually transport one, so the
   436	        # manifest attests truthfully. Any LiveContextViolation PROPAGATES (fail
   437	        # closed, no fallback rendering). F9: never pass a '-breaking-'
   438	        # harness_version here (see assemble_live docstring).
   439	        declared_system_prompt = (
   440	            self.system_prompt if self.adapter.sends_system_prompt else ""
   441	        )
   442	        drafts = _build_drafts(task, system_prompt=declared_system_prompt)
   443	        assembly = assemble_live(
   444	            drafts,
   445	            budget_tokens=budget_for(self.tier),
   446	            model_id=self.model,
   447	            harness_version="metaharness:0.1.0",
   448	            tier=self.tier,
   449	        )
   450	        prompt = assembly.prompt
   451	        try:
   452	            emit_run_event(
   453	                "context.manifest",
   454	                {
   455	                    "schema_version": 1,
   456	                    "shadow": False,
   457	                    "task_id": task.id,
   458	                    "round": 0,
   459	                    "live_messages_hash": content_hash(prompt),
   460	                    "manifest": assembly.manifest.model_dump(mode="json"),
   461	                },
   462	            )
   463	        except Exception:
   464	            # Telemetry cannot fail the model call (only emit is guarded).
   465	            pass
   466	        # the CLI argv receives the assembler's REDACTED system prompt, never
   467	        # worker.system_prompt raw (F3).
   468	        argv, stdin_text = self.adapter.build(self, prompt, assembly.system_prompt, workspace)
   469	        # Carry the full outer-host chain into nested harnesses. This blocks
   470	        # direct recursion and cycles such as Codex -> Pi -> Codex before spawn.
   471	        env = {
   472	            **os.environ,
   473	            **self.extra_env,
   474	            **child_host_environment(self.cli),
   475	        }
   476	
   477	        try:
   478	            proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
   479	                *argv,
   480	                cwd=workspace,
   481	                env=env,
   482	                # Coding CLIs routinely spawn shells, tests, and helper agents.
   483	                # Give the attempt its own group so timeout/cancellation cannot
   484	                # leave descendants mutating the workspace after escalation.
   485	                start_new_session=True,
   486	                stdin=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE if stdin_text is not None else asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   487	                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   488	                stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   489	            )
   490	        except OSError as exc:
   491	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: cannot launch '{self.binary}': {exc}") from exc
   492	
   493	        eff = self.effective_timeout_s(task)
   494	        try:
   495	            stdout_b, stderr_b = await asyncio.wait_for(
   496	                proc.communicate(stdin_text.encode() if stdin_text is not None else None),
   497	                timeout=eff,
   498	            )
   499	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   500	            await self._terminate_process_group(proc)
   501	            # :g not :.0f — subsecond test timeouts (e.g. 0.5) must not render as "0s"
   502	            raise WorkerTimeout(f"{self.cli}: timed out after {eff:g}s", timeout_s=eff)
   503	        except asyncio.CancelledError:
   504	            await asyncio.shield(self._terminate_process_group(proc))
   505	            raise
   506	
   507	        stdout = stdout_b.decode(errors="replace")
   508	        stderr = stderr_b.decode(errors="replace")
   509	        if proc.returncode != 0:
   510	            detail = (stderr or stdout).strip()[-2000:]
   511	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: exit {proc.returncode}: {detail}")
   512	
   513	        text, cost = self.adapter.parse(stdout)
   514	        from metaharness.harness.local import parse_output
   515	        # F3 (panel 2026-07-09, GLM P2): coding CLIs (codex/opencode) report cost
   516	        # 0.0 and no token usage, so CodeProposer charged ~nothing for the most
   517	        # expensive calls in the harness. No adapter surfaces a token count today,
   518	        # so ESTIMATE from character length (~4 chars/token) — a rough but non-zero
   519	        # figure so budget accounting reflects that these calls are not free.
   520	        tokens_in = len(prompt) // 4
   521	        tokens_out = len(text) // 4
   522	        return WorkerResult(
   523	            task_id=task.id,
   524	            worker_id=self.worker_id,
   525	            tier=self.tier,
   526	            model=self.model,
   527	            output=parse_output(text, expect_json=bool(task.output_schema)),
   528	            raw_text=text,
   529	            tokens_in=tokens_in,
   530	            tokens_out=tokens_out,
   531	            cost_usd=cost,
   532	            workspace_root=str(workspace),
   533	        )
   534	
   535	    @staticmethod
   536	    async def _terminate_process_group(proc: asyncio.subprocess.Process) -> None:
   537	        """Terminate and reap an attempt's complete POSIX process group."""
   538	        if proc.returncode is not None:
   539	            await proc.wait()
   540	            return
   541	        pgid = CodingAgentWorker._process_group_id(proc)
   542	        tracked = CodingAgentWorker._linux_descendant_pids(proc.pid)
   543	        CodingAgentWorker._signal_process_tree(proc, signal.SIGTERM, pgid, tracked)
   544	        try:
   545	            await asyncio.wait_for(proc.wait(), timeout=0.5)
   546	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   547	            pass
   548	        await asyncio.sleep(0.05)
   549	        tracked.update(CodingAgentWorker._linux_descendant_pids(proc.pid))
   550	        if (
   551	            proc.returncode is not None
   552	            and not CodingAgentWorker._group_alive(pgid)
   553	            and not CodingAgentWorker._any_pid_alive(tracked)
   554	        ):
   555	            return
   556	        CodingAgentWorker._signal_process_tree(proc, signal.SIGKILL, pgid, tracked)
   557	        try:
   558	            await asyncio.wait_for(proc.wait(), timeout=2.0)
   559	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   560	            if proc.returncode is None:
   561	                proc.kill()
   562	                await proc.wait()
   563	
   564	    @staticmethod
   565	    def _process_group_id(proc: asyncio.subprocess.Process) -> int | None:
   566	        try:
   567	            return os.getpgid(proc.pid)
   568	        except (ProcessLookupError, PermissionError, OSError):
   569	            return proc.pid
   570	
     1	"""TaskExecutor: the execute→verify→reflect→escalate loop for one task.
     2	
     3	This is the heart of the meta-harness. One call runs a task to completion:
     4	
     5	    route (cheapest capable) → run → confirm authenticity → verify →
     6	    on FAIL: reflect, retry timeout once in-tier, otherwise escalate → record everything
     7	
     8	Every attempt updates the capability matrix (verified outcomes only), charges
     9	the budget, and is journaled into the provenance chain under the orchestrator's
    10	own key. Guardrails from core.budget stop runaway loops: hard budget ceilings,
    11	plateau detection across attempts, and step-repetition dedup.
    12	"""
    13	from __future__ import annotations
    14	
    15	import asyncio
    16	import time
    17	from typing import Any, Awaitable, Callable, Optional
    18	
    19	from metaharness.core.budget import Budget, BudgetExceeded, PlateauDetector, action_signature
    20	from metaharness.core.types import (
    21	    Attempt,
    22	    MASTMode,
    23	    Task,
    24	    TaskOutcome,
    25	    TaskType,
    26	    Tier,
    27	    VerificationResult,
    28	    Verdict,
    29	    WorkerResult,
    30	    now,
    31	)
    32	from metaharness.evals.execution import (
    33	    run_workspace_execution,
    34	    verify_code_edit_execution,
    35	)
    36	from metaharness.evals.verifiers import authenticity_failure, verify_output
    37	from metaharness.harness.runner import verify_result
    38	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    39	from metaharness.identity.provenance import ProvenanceLog
    40	from metaharness.identity.registry import WorkerRegistry
    41	from metaharness.observability.tracing import tracer
    42	from metaharness.observability.run_events import (
    43	    bind_run_event_sink,
    44	    reset_run_event_sink,
    45	)
    46	from metaharness.routing.router import TIER_ORDER, Router
    47	
    48	# a reflector turns a failed attempt into advice for the next one
    49	Reflector = Callable[[Task, Attempt], Optional[str]]
    50	# a judge grades an UNVERIFIED output against its contract (rubric-judge slot
    51	# of the verifier hierarchy); async because it calls a worker
    52	Judge = Callable[..., "object"]
    53	ExecutionVerifier = Callable[
    54	    [Task, WorkerResult], Awaitable[Optional[VerificationResult]]
    55	]
    56	WorkspaceVerifier = Callable[[str], Awaitable[Optional[VerificationResult]]]
    57	TaskEventSink = Callable[[str, dict[str, Any]], None]
    58	
    59	
    60	class TaskExecutor:
    61	    def __init__(
    62	        self,
    63	        router: Router,
    64	        registry: Optional[WorkerRegistry] = None,
    65	        provenance: Optional[ProvenanceLog] = None,
    66	        orchestrator_keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
    67	        budget: Optional[Budget] = None,
    68	        reflector: Optional[Reflector] = None,
    69	        playbook_hints: Optional[Callable[[Task], list[str]]] = None,
    70	        observer: Optional[Callable[[TaskOutcome], None]] = None,
    71	        judge: Optional[Judge] = None,
    72	        execution_verifier: Optional[ExecutionVerifier] = verify_code_edit_execution,
    73	        workspace_root: str = "",
    74	        workspace_verifier: Optional[WorkspaceVerifier] = run_workspace_execution,
    75	    ) -> None:
    76	        self.router = router
    77	        self.registry = registry
    78	        self.provenance = provenance
    79	        self.orchestrator_keypair = orchestrator_keypair
    80	        self.budget = budget
    81	        self.reflector = reflector
    82	        self.playbook_hints = playbook_hints
    83	        self.observer = observer
    84	        self.judge = judge
    85	        self.execution_verifier = execution_verifier
    86	        self.workspace_root = workspace_root
    87	        self.workspace_verifier = workspace_verifier
    88	        if provenance is not None and orchestrator_keypair is None:
    89	            raise ValueError("provenance logging needs the orchestrator keypair")
    90	
    91	    def _record(self, action: str, detail: dict) -> None:
    92	        if self.provenance is not None:
    93	            self.provenance.append(
    94	                "orchestrator", action, detail, keypair=self.orchestrator_keypair
    95	            )
    96	
    97	    def _attempt_task(self, task: Task, advice: list[str]) -> Task:
    98	        """The task as sent for this attempt — original contract plus accumulated
    99	        reflections/playbook hints in `advice`.
   100	
   101	        META-19 (F2): advice lands in `task.advice`, NOT `task.boundaries`.
   102	        Reflexion/selflearn text quotes prior worker output and retrieved
   103	        content verbatim; folding it into boundaries laundered untrusted data
   104	        into a caller-authored instruction contract. The worker renders advice
   105	        as untrusted-derived feedback, never as an instruction slot.
   106	        """
   107	        if not advice:
   108	            return task
   109	        variant = task.model_copy(deep=True)
   110	        variant.advice = list(task.advice) + advice
   111	        return variant
   112	
   113	    async def execute(
   114	        self, task: Task, *, event_sink: Optional[TaskEventSink] = None
   115	    ) -> TaskOutcome:
   116	        """Execute one task, optionally emitting live attempt/verification events.
   117	
   118	        The callback is synchronous by design: the workflow journal fsyncs each
   119	        event before execution moves past the corresponding transition.
   120	        """
   121	        def emit(kind: str, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
   122	            if event_sink is not None:
   123	                event_sink(kind, payload)
   124	
   125	        outcome = TaskOutcome(task=task)
   126	        plateau = PlateauDetector()
   127	        seen_signatures: set[str] = set()
   128	        excluded_tiers: set[Tier] = set()
   129	        # A timeout is an operational signal, not evidence that the tier lacks
   130	        # capability. Give each routed tier one retry before excluding it; the
   131	        # set keeps repeated timeouts from turning max_attempts into an
   132	        # unbounded same-tier loop (issue #11).
   133	        timeout_retry_used: set[Tier] = set()
   134	        forced_retry_tier: Optional[Tier] = None
   135	        advice: list[str] = []
   136	        execution_evidence_latency_s = 0.0
   137	        if task.requires_execution_evidence:
   138	            evidence_started = time.monotonic()
   139	            evidence = None
   140	            if self.workspace_root and self.workspace_verifier is not None:
   141	                try:
   142	                    evidence = await self.workspace_verifier(self.workspace_root)
   143	                except Exception as exc:  # infrastructure uncertainty is evidence too
   144	                    self._record("execution.evidence_error", {
   145	                        "task_id": task.id,
   146	                        "error": f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"[:300],
   147	                    })
   148	            execution_evidence_latency_s = time.monotonic() - evidence_started
   149	            variant = task.model_copy(deep=True)
   150	            if evidence is None:
   151	                receipt = (
   152	                    "Harness-owned execution receipt: no approved runnable test "
   153	                    "command was discovered or no OS sandbox was available. Do not "
   154	                    "claim command-based acceptance criteria are met."
   155	                )
   156	            else:
   157	                receipt = (
   158	                    "Harness-owned execution receipt (not worker-authored):\n"
   159	                    f"{evidence.detail}"
   160	                )
   161	            variant.inputs["harness_execution_evidence"] = receipt
   162	            task_for_attempts = variant
   163	            self._record("execution.evidence_attached", {
   164	                "task_id": task.id,
   165	                "available": evidence is not None,
   166	                "verdict": evidence.verdict.value if evidence is not None else None,
   167	            })
   168	        else:
   169	            task_for_attempts = task
   170	        if self.playbook_hints:
   171	            # off the event loop: knowledge-pack hints may embed the query
   172	            # over the network (blocking HTTP), and a cold endpoint would
   173	            # otherwise stall every run on the loop for up to its timeout
   174	            advice.extend(await asyncio.to_thread(self.playbook_hints, task))
   175	
   176	        with tracer().start_as_current_span("task.execute") as span:
   177	            span.set_attribute("task.id", task.id)
   178	            span.set_attribute("task.type", task.task_type.value)
   179	            self._record("task.started", {"task_id": task.id, "objective": task.objective[:200]})
   180	
   181	            for n in range(1, task.max_attempts + 1):
   182	                route_exclusions = excluded_tiers
   183	                if forced_retry_tier is not None:
   184	                    # One-shot exact-tier retry. Merely leaving the tier
   185	                    # available is insufficient: after charging the timed-out
   186	                    # attempt, Router's affordability filter could otherwise
   187	                    # select a different (usually cheaper) tier.
   188	                    route_exclusions = excluded_tiers | {
   189	                        tier for tier in TIER_ORDER if tier != forced_retry_tier
   190	                    }
   191	                    forced_retry_tier = None
   192	                try:
   193	                    decision = self.router.decide(
   194	                        task, exclude=route_exclusions, budget=self.budget
   195	                    )
   196	                except ValueError as exc:
   197	                    self._record("task.aborted", {"task_id": task.id, "reason": str(exc)})
   198	                    # Routing failure is a real execution failure.  Leaving the
   199	                    # default UNVERIFIED verdict here used to let WorkflowEngine
   200	                    # record a zero-attempt step as completed.
   201	                    outcome.final_verdict = Verdict.FAIL
   202	                    break
   203	
   204	                variant = self._attempt_task(task_for_attempts, advice)
   205	                runner = self.router.runner_for(decision)
   206	                assignment = {
   207	                    "n": n,
   208	                    "worker_id": decision.worker_id,
   209	                    "model": decision.model,
   210	                    "tier": decision.tier.value,
   211	                    "requested_role": task.role,
   212	                    "requested_capabilities": list(task.required_capabilities),
   213	                    "requested_worker_id": task.worker_id,
   214	                }
   215	                emit("attempt.assigned", assignment)
   216	                emit("attempt.started", assignment)
   217	                tool_event_sink = (
   218	                    (lambda kind, payload: emit(kind, {"n": n, **payload}))
   219	                    if event_sink is not None else None
   220	                )
   221	                event_token = bind_run_event_sink(tool_event_sink)
   222	                try:
   223	                    result = await runner.run(variant)
   224	                finally:
   225	                    reset_run_event_sink(event_token)
   226	                result.task_id = task.id
   227	                emit("verification.started", {
   228	                    **assignment,
   229	                    "worker_id": result.worker_id,
   230	                    "model": result.model,
   231	                    "tier": result.tier.value,
   232	                })
   233	
   234	                # charge always, fail truthfully (issue #5): the deterministic
   235	                # verification (authenticity, then verify_output) is computed
   236	                # BEFORE the charge so a genuine worker malfunction is already
   237	                # known when the budget check below decides whether to mask it.
   238	                # The rubric-judge slot stays AFTER the charge — an over-budget
   239	                # attempt must stop before paying for an extra LLM judge call.
   240	                signature_verified = (
   241	                    self.registry is not None and verify_result(result, self.registry)
   242	                )
   243	                if self.registry is not None and not signature_verified:
   244	                    verification = authenticity_failure(
   245	                        f"result from {result.worker_id!r} has no valid signature "
   246	                        "under its registered key"
   247	                    )
   248	                    worker_malfunctioned = True
   249	                else:
   250	                    verification = verify_output(task, result)
   251	                    worker_malfunctioned = bool(result.error)
   252	                # Issue #1: the workspace selector itself must be covered by a
   253	                # verified v2 signature. Legacy v1 roots remain readable for
   254	                # history but never select code for execution.
   255	                workspace_attested = (
   256	                    signature_verified and result.signature_version >= 2
   257	                )
   258	                if (
   259	                    task.task_type == TaskType.CODE_EDIT
   260	                    and result.workspace_root
   261	                    and not workspace_attested
   262	                ):
   263	                    self._record("execution.skipped", {
   264	                        "task_id": task.id,
   265	                        "attempt": n,
   266	                        "reason": "workspace_root is not covered by a verified v2 signature",
   267	                    })
   268	
   269	                try:
   270	                    if self.budget is not None:
   271	                        self.budget.charge(
   272	                            cost_usd=result.cost_usd,
   273	                            tokens=result.tokens_in + result.tokens_out,
   274	                            wall_s=result.latency_s + (
   275	                                execution_evidence_latency_s if n == 1 else 0.0
   276	                            ),
   277	                        )
   278	                except BudgetExceeded as exc:
   279	                    # a genuine worker malfunction (result.error or an
   280	                    # authenticity failure) always wins over budget-exhausted —
   281	                    # keep the verification already computed above. A mere
   282	                    # low-score verify-FAIL is NOT a masked failure; that case
   283	                    # keeps today's budget-FAIL verification exactly.
   284	                    if not worker_malfunctioned:
   285	                        verification = VerificationResult(
   286	                            verdict=Verdict.FAIL, score=0.0, detail=str(exc),
   287	                            failure_mode=MASTMode.BUDGET_EXCEEDED, scorer="budget",
   288	                        )
   289	                    emit("verification.completed", self._verification_event(
   290	                        n, result, verification
   291	                    ))
   292	                    outcome.attempts.append(Attempt(n=n, result=result, verification=verification))
   293	                    self._record("task.budget_exceeded", {"task_id": task.id, "detail": str(exc)})
   294	                    break
   295	
   296	                # Execution/tests are stronger evidence than output narration
   297	                # or a text success_check, but stay AFTER the worker budget gate:
   298	                # an already-over-budget attempt must not launch another process.
   299	                if (
   300	                    workspace_attested
   301	                    and self.execution_verifier is not None
   302	                    and not result.error
   303	                    and verification.scorer != "schema"
   304	                ):
   305	                    execution_started = time.monotonic()
   306	                    try:
   307	                        execution = await self.execution_verifier(variant, result)
   308	                    except Exception as exc:  # verifier infrastructure is not model failure
   309	                        execution = None
   310	                        self._record("execution.error", {
   311	                            "task_id": task.id,
   312	                            "attempt": n,
   313	                            "error": f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"[:300],
   314	                        })
   315	                    execution_latency_s = time.monotonic() - execution_started
   316	                    if execution is not None:
   317	                        execution.latency_s = execution_latency_s
   318	                        verification = execution
   319	                    try:
   320	                        if self.budget is not None:
   321	                            self.budget.charge(wall_s=execution_latency_s)
   322	                    except BudgetExceeded as exc:
   323	                        verification = VerificationResult(
   324	                            verdict=Verdict.FAIL, score=0.0, detail=str(exc),
   325	                            failure_mode=MASTMode.BUDGET_EXCEEDED, scorer="budget",
   326	                        )
   327	                        emit("verification.completed", self._verification_event(
   328	                            n, result, verification
   329	                        ))
   330	                        outcome.attempts.append(
   331	                            Attempt(n=n, result=result, verification=verification)
   332	                        )
   333	                        self._record("task.budget_exceeded", {
   334	                            "task_id": task.id, "detail": str(exc),
   335	                        })
   336	                        break
   337	
   338	                if (verification.verdict == Verdict.UNVERIFIED
   339	                        and self.judge is not None
   340	                        and task.task_type != TaskType.PLANNING):
   341	                    # rubric-judge slot: no deterministic check exists, so a
   342	                    # fresh-context LLM grades the output against the step's
   343	                    # own contract — a FAIL enters the normal retry loop
   344	                    # BEFORE any dependent step consumes the output
   345	                    try:
   346	                        judge_result = result
   347	                        if result.workspace_root and not (
   348	                            signature_verified and result.signature_version >= 2
   349	                        ):
   350	                            # Evidence collection reads files. Apply the same
   351	                            # attestation rule as execution so a legacy signed
   352	                            # result cannot redirect the judge into arbitrary
   353	                            # host paths.
   354	                            judge_result = result.model_copy(
   355	                                update={"workspace_root": ""}
   356	                            )
   357	                        verification = await self.judge(variant, judge_result)
   358	                    except BudgetExceeded as exc:
   359	                        # the judge call's own worker spend is charged against
   360	                        # the same budget (make_judge) — a budget stop here
   361	                        # must surface as a budget stop, never be laundered
   362	                        # into a "broken judge" note.
   363	                        verification = VerificationResult(
   364	                            verdict=Verdict.FAIL, score=0.0, detail=str(exc),
   365	                            failure_mode=MASTMode.BUDGET_EXCEEDED, scorer="budget",
   366	                        )
   367	                        emit("verification.completed", self._verification_event(
   368	                            n, result, verification
   369	                        ))
   370	                        outcome.attempts.append(Attempt(n=n, result=result, verification=verification))
   371	                        self._record("task.budget_exceeded", {"task_id": task.id, "detail": str(exc)})
   372	                        break
   373	                    except Exception as exc:  # a broken judge must never fail the task,
   374	                        # but a silent one is undiagnosable — record why it broke
   375	                        self._record("judge.error", {
   376	                            "task_id": task.id, "attempt": n,
   377	                            "error": f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}"[:300],
   378	                        })
   379	                timeout_failure = (
   380	                    verification.verdict == Verdict.FAIL
   381	                    and verification.failure_mode == MASTMode.TIMEOUT
   382	                )
   383	
   384	                # capability matrix learns from checkable outcomes only
   385	                # (deterministic or rubric-judged; scorer says which). An
   386	                # authenticity failure says nothing about the model's SKILL and
   387	                # must never be recorded (verifiers.authenticity_failure
   388	                # invariant) — pre-issue-#5 this was enforced by nesting; the
   389	                # reorder flattened it, so guard on the scorer (panel P1).
   390	                # A timeout is likewise neutral: it says the attempt exhausted
   391	                # its wall-clock allowance, not that the model could not solve
   392	                # the task. A later PASS still earns normal positive evidence.
   393	                # META-19 (F6): a context-contract violation is a deterministic
   394	                # harness failure, not evidence about the model's skill — never
   395	                # bank it in the capability matrix / routing evidence.
   396	                context_contract_failure = result.error_kind == "context_contract"
   397	                if (verification.verdict in (Verdict.PASS, Verdict.FAIL)
   398	                        and verification.scorer != "authenticity"
   399	                        and not timeout_failure
   400	                        and not context_contract_failure):
   401	                    self.router.matrix.record(
   402	                        result.model, task.task_type, verification.verdict == Verdict.PASS
   403	                    )
   404	
   405	                attempt = Attempt(n=n, result=result, verification=verification)
   406	                emit("verification.completed", self._verification_event(
   407	                    n, result, verification
   408	                ))
   409	                outcome.attempts.append(attempt)
   410	                outcome.total_cost_usd += result.cost_usd
   411	                self._record(
   412	                    "task.attempt",
   413	                    {
   414	                        "task_id": task.id, "n": n, "tier": decision.tier.value,
   415	                        "model": result.model, "verdict": verification.verdict.value,
   416	                        "detail": verification.detail[:200],
   417	                        "worker_signature": result.signature_b64,
   418	                        "worker_signature_version": result.signature_version,
   419	                        # issue #2: parity with the step.attempt journal payload
   420	                        "failure_mode": (verification.failure_mode.value
     1	"""Shared domain types for the meta-harness.
     2	
     3	These are the vocabulary the whole system speaks: tasks flow in, get routed to a
     4	capability tier, executed by a worker harness, verified, and (on failure) reflected
     5	on. Everything is a plain pydantic model so it serializes cleanly into the journal,
     6	the provenance log, and the WebUI API.
     7	"""
     8	from __future__ import annotations
     9	
    10	import time
    11	import uuid
    12	from enum import Enum
    13	from typing import Any, Optional
    14	
    15	from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, model_validator
    16	
    17	
    18	def _new_id(prefix: str) -> str:
    19	    return f"{prefix}_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"
    20	
    21	
    22	def now() -> float:
    23	    return time.time()
    24	
    25	
    26	class Tier(str, Enum):
    27	    """Capability tiers. The router picks the cheapest tier likely to succeed and
    28	    escalates on a verifiable failure signal."""
    29	
    30	    SMALL = "small"    # haiku / 8B-class: narrow, verifiable, single-pass work
    31	    MID = "mid"        # sonnet-class: multi-step but bounded
    32	    FRONTIER = "frontier"  # opus/fable-class: long-horizon, ambiguous, novel
    33	
    34	
    35	class TaskType(str, Enum):
    36	    """Coarse task taxonomy. Drives the capability matrix and the enrichment stack.
    37	    A prescribed workflow tags each step with one of these."""
    38	
    39	    CLASSIFY = "classify"
    40	    EXTRACT = "extract"
    41	    SUMMARIZE = "summarize"
    42	    TRANSFORM = "transform"
    43	    ARITHMETIC = "arithmetic"      # always tool-offloaded to code
    44	    CODE_EDIT = "code_edit"
    45	    REASONING = "reasoning"
    46	    PLANNING = "planning"
    47	    GENERAL = "general"
    48	
    49	
    50	class Verdict(str, Enum):
    51	    PASS = "pass"
    52	    FAIL = "fail"
    53	    UNVERIFIED = "unverified"      # no scorer could produce ground truth
    54	
    55	
    56	class MASTMode(str, Enum):
    57	    """Failure vocabulary from the MAST taxonomy (Berkeley, 2025). Used to label
    58	    failures consistently so the learning loop can cluster before fixing."""
    59	
    60	    # system / specification design (~44% of MAS failures)
    61	    DISOBEY_TASK_SPEC = "disobey_task_spec"
    62	    DISOBEY_ROLE_SPEC = "disobey_role_spec"
    63	    STEP_REPETITION = "step_repetition"
    64	    LOSE_HISTORY = "lose_history"
    65	    UNAWARE_TERMINATION = "unaware_termination"
    66	    # inter-agent misalignment (~32%)
    67	    IGNORE_INPUT = "ignore_input"
    68	    WITHHELD_INFO = "withheld_info"
    69	    MISMATCHED_ASSUMPTION = "mismatched_assumption"
    70	    # task verification & termination
    71	    PREMATURE_TERMINATION = "premature_termination"
    72	    NO_VERIFICATION = "no_verification"
    73	    INCORRECT_VERIFICATION = "incorrect_verification"
    74	    # operational (harness-level)
    75	    TOOL_ERROR = "tool_error"
    76	    SCHEMA_INVALID = "schema_invalid"
    77	    BUDGET_EXCEEDED = "budget_exceeded"
    78	    TIMEOUT = "timeout"          # issue #2: distinct from generic TOOL_ERROR
    79	    UNKNOWN = "unknown"
    80	
    81	
    82	class Task(BaseModel):
    83	    """A unit of work handed to a worker harness."""
    84	
    85	    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: _new_id("task"))
    86	    task_type: TaskType = TaskType.GENERAL
    87	    # explicit delegation contract (Anthropic multi-agent lesson): objective,
    88	    # output format, and boundaries are load-bearing, not decoration.
    89	    objective: str = ""
    90	    inputs: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    91	    output_schema: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None
    92	    boundaries: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    93	    # META-19 (F2): accumulated reflections/knowledge hints, carried SEPARATELY
    94	    # from `boundaries`. Advice quotes prior worker output and retrieved content
    95	    # verbatim, so it is untrusted-derived and must never render into an
    96	    # instruction slot the way caller-authored boundaries do.
    97	    advice: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    98	    # a checkable success signal, if one exists. Interpreted by the verifier.
    99	    success_check: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None
   100	    tier_hint: Optional[Tier] = None
   101	    # Human-friendly assignment constraints. ``worker_id`` is a hard pin;
   102	    # role/capabilities are requirements that any selected worker must satisfy.
   103	    role: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, exclude_if=lambda value: value is None)
   104	    required_capabilities: list[str] = Field(
   105	        default_factory=list, exclude_if=lambda value: not value
   106	    )
   107	    worker_id: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, exclude_if=lambda value: value is None)
   108	    max_attempts: int = 3
   109	    # tool names this task may call (small per-step subset, never the catalog)
   110	    tools: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
   111	    # Ask the orchestrator to attach a harness-owned, sandboxed test receipt.
   112	    # This never grants the worker a command-execution tool.
   113	    requires_execution_evidence: bool = False
   114	
   115	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   116	    def _assignment_is_unambiguous(self) -> "Task":
   117	        self.role = (self.role.strip() or None) if self.role else None
   118	        self.worker_id = (self.worker_id.strip() or None) if self.worker_id else None
   119	        self.required_capabilities = list(dict.fromkeys(
   120	            value.strip() for value in self.required_capabilities if value.strip()
   121	        ))
   122	        if self.worker_id and self.tier_hint is not None:
   123	            raise ValueError("worker_id and tier_hint cannot be combined")
   124	        return self
   125	
   126	
   127	class WorkerResult(BaseModel):
   128	    """What a worker harness returns for one attempt."""
   129	
   130	    task_id: str
   131	    worker_id: str
   132	    tier: Tier
   133	    model: str
   134	    output: Any = None
   135	    raw_text: str = ""
   136	    tool_calls: list[dict[str, Any]] = Field(default_factory=list)
   137	    tokens_in: int = 0
   138	    tokens_out: int = 0
   139	    cost_usd: float = 0.0
   140	    latency_s: float = 0.0
   141	    error: Optional[str] = None
   142	    # META-19 (F6): coarse classification of `error` for control flow. A
   143	    # deterministic context-contract violation ("context_contract") is not a
   144	    # model-capability signal — the executor aborts retries and excludes it from
   145	    # routing evidence. Other failures keep None (behavior unchanged).
   146	    error_kind: Optional[str] = None
   147	    # Legacy v1 signatures covered only the worker's textual result. New v2
   148	    # signatures also attest the execution-relevant metadata below. Keeping an
   149	    # explicit version lets old journal signatures remain verifiable without
   150	    # allowing their unsigned workspace_root to select code for execution.
   151	    signature_version: int = 1
   152	    # Derived metadata (issue #2): set by BaseRunner.run when `error` came from
   153	    # a WorkerTimeout. It is covered by v2 signatures.
   154	    timed_out: bool = False
   155	    # the directory this worker's file side-effects land in (builtin tool jail
   156	    # root or coding-CLI cwd), recorded by the runner that KNOWS it — evidence
   157	    # collection and run packaging must never infer this from cwd or guess
   158	    workspace_root: str = ""
   159	    # detached signature over `result_signing_bytes(...)`, made with the worker's
   160	    # registered key, so the orchestrator can confirm who produced this result.
   161	    signature_b64: Optional[str] = None
   162	
   163	
   164	class VerificationResult(BaseModel):
   165	    verdict: Verdict
   166	    score: float = 0.0            # 0..1
   167	    detail: str = ""
   168	    failure_mode: Optional[MASTMode] = None
   169	    scorer: str = ""             # which scorer produced this (execution/schema/judge)
   170	    latency_s: float = 0.0        # verifier wall time; execution checks charge this to Budget
   171	
   172	
   173	class Attempt(BaseModel):
   174	    """One pass through execute+verify. A task may take several before it passes
   175	    or exhausts its budget."""
   176	
   177	    n: int
   178	    result: WorkerResult
   179	    verification: VerificationResult
   180	    reflection: Optional[str] = None   # written only after a failed attempt
   181	
   182	
   183	class TaskOutcome(BaseModel):
   184	    """The full record for a task: every attempt and the final disposition."""
   185	
   186	    task: Task
   187	    attempts: list[Attempt] = Field(default_factory=list)
   188	    final_verdict: Verdict = Verdict.UNVERIFIED
   189	    final_output: Any = None
   190	    total_cost_usd: float = 0.0
   191	    escalations: int = 0
   192	    started_at: float = Field(default_factory=now)
   193	    ended_at: Optional[float] = None
     1	"""Durable, append-only workflow run events.
     2	
     3	New runs write one versioned canonical stream.  ``entries()`` is an explicit
     4	projection onto the historical ``JournalEntry`` vocabulary so existing package,
     5	harvest, and web readers remain compatible without duplicate on-disk records.
     6	"""
     7	from __future__ import annotations
     8	
     9	import contextlib
    10	import json
    11	import math
    12	import os
    13	import stat
    14	import time
    15	from pathlib import Path
    16	from typing import Any, Iterator, Literal, Optional
    17	
    18	import fcntl
    19	from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, field_validator, model_validator
    20	
    21	
    22	CANONICAL_KINDS = frozenset({
    23	    "run.started", "step.ready", "step.started",
    24	    "attempt.assigned", "attempt.started",
    25	    "tool.requested", "tool.completed",
    26	    "verification.started", "verification.completed",
    27	    "approval.required", "approval.resolved",
    28	    "step.completed", "step.failed", "step.skipped",
    29	    "run.completed", "run.failed",
    30	    # META-19: the live context manifest journaled per attempt round — the
    31	    # authoritative "what did the model see" record. Attempt-scoped (the
    32	    # executor sink merges the attempt number `n`), no legacy projection.
    33	    "context.manifest",
    34	})
    35	
    36	
    37	class RunEvent(BaseModel):
    38	    """One event in the canonical v1 run stream."""
    39	
    40	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
    41	    seq: int = Field(ge=0)
    42	    at: float
    43	    kind: str
    44	    run_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
    45	    snapshot_digest: str = Field(pattern=r"^[0-9a-f]{64}$")
    46	    step_id: Optional[str] = None
    47	    attempt_id: Optional[str] = None
    48	    payload: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    49	
    50	    model_config = {"extra": "forbid"}
    51	
    52	    @field_validator("at")
    53	    @classmethod
    54	    def _finite_timestamp(cls, value: float) -> float:
    55	        if not math.isfinite(value):
    56	            raise ValueError("event timestamp must be finite")
    57	        return value
    58	
    59	    @field_validator("kind")
    60	    @classmethod
    61	    def _known_kind(cls, value: str) -> str:
    62	        if value not in CANONICAL_KINDS:
    63	            raise ValueError(f"unknown canonical event kind {value!r}")
    64	        return value
    65	
    66	    @model_validator(mode="after")
    67	    def _required_identity_fields(self) -> "RunEvent":
    68	        if self.kind.startswith("run."):
    69	            if self.step_id is not None or self.attempt_id is not None:
    70	                raise ValueError("run events cannot carry step/attempt IDs")
    71	        elif not self.step_id:
    72	            raise ValueError(f"{self.kind} requires a step ID")
    73	        if self.kind.startswith(("attempt.", "tool.", "verification.")):
    74	            if not self.attempt_id:
    75	                raise ValueError(f"{self.kind} requires an attempt ID")
    76	        return self
    77	
    78	
    79	class JournalEntry(BaseModel):
    80	    """Historical event shape returned by :meth:`Journal.entries`.
    81	
    82	    It intentionally keeps the old permissive defaults because archived
    83	    journals with omitted ``step_id``/``payload`` remain valid inputs.
    84	    """
    85	
    86	    seq: int
    87	    at: float
    88	    kind: str
    89	    run_id: str
    90	    step_id: Optional[str] = None
    91	    payload: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    92	
    93	
    94	def _reject_duplicate_keys(pairs: list[tuple[str, Any]]) -> dict[str, Any]:
    95	    result: dict[str, Any] = {}
    96	    for key, value in pairs:
    97	        if key in result:
    98	            raise ValueError(f"duplicate JSON key {key!r}")
    99	        result[key] = value
   100	    return result
   101	
   102	
   103	def _reject_constant(value: str) -> None:
   104	    raise ValueError(f"non-finite JSON number {value}")
   105	
   106	
   107	def _parse_line(line: str, *, line_no: int) -> dict[str, Any]:
   108	    try:
   109	        value = json.loads(
   110	            line,
   111	            object_pairs_hook=_reject_duplicate_keys,
   112	            parse_constant=_reject_constant,
   113	        )
   114	    except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as exc:
   115	        raise ValueError(f"invalid journal JSON at line {line_no}: {exc}") from exc
   116	    if not isinstance(value, dict):
   117	        raise ValueError(f"journal line {line_no} must be a JSON object")
   118	    return value
   119	
   120	
   121	def _legacy_projection(event: RunEvent) -> Optional[JournalEntry]:
   122	    kind = event.kind
   123	    payload = dict(event.payload)
   124	    projected: Optional[str]
   125	    if kind in {"run.started", "step.started"}:
   126	        projected = kind
   127	    elif kind == "verification.completed":
   128	        projected = "step.attempt"
   129	    elif kind == "approval.required":
   130	        projected = "hitl.requested"
   131	    elif kind == "approval.resolved":
   132	        projected = "hitl.resolved"
   133	    elif kind in {"step.completed", "step.failed", "step.skipped"}:
   134	        projected = kind
   135	    elif kind in {"run.completed", "run.failed"}:
   136	        projected = "run.finished"
   137	        payload.setdefault("status", "completed" if kind == "run.completed" else "failed")
   138	    else:
   139	        projected = None
   140	    if projected is None:
   141	        return None
   142	    return JournalEntry(
   143	        seq=event.seq,
   144	        at=event.at,
   145	        kind=projected,
   146	        run_id=event.run_id,
   147	        step_id=event.step_id,
   148	        payload=payload,
   149	    )
   150	
   151	
   152	def _validate_canonical_history(events: list[RunEvent]) -> None:
   153	    if not events:
   154	        return
   155	    if events[0].kind != "run.started":
   156	        raise ValueError("canonical journal must begin with run.started")
   157	    if sum(event.kind == "run.started" for event in events) != 1:
   158	        raise ValueError("canonical journal must contain one run.started")
   159	    terminals = [event for event in events if event.kind in {"run.completed", "run.failed"}]
   160	    if len(terminals) > 1:
   161	        raise ValueError("canonical journal has duplicate run terminal events")
   162	    if terminals and events[-1] is not terminals[0]:
   163	        raise ValueError("canonical journal has events after its run terminal")
   164	    step_terminals: set[str] = set()
   165	    for event in events:
   166	        if event.kind in {"step.completed", "step.failed", "step.skipped"}:
   167	            assert event.step_id is not None
   168	            if event.step_id in step_terminals:
   169	                raise ValueError(
   170	                    f"canonical journal has duplicate terminal for step {event.step_id!r}"
   171	                )
   172	            step_terminals.add(event.step_id)
   173	
   174	
   175	class Journal:
   176	    """A strict durable journal with a legacy compatibility mode.
   177	
   178	    Engine-created journals are canonical.  Direct callers using ``append``
   179	    keep the historical shape, which is useful for archived fixtures.  A file
   180	    may never mix the two formats.
   181	    """
   182	
   183	    def __init__(self, path: Optional[str | Path] = None, *, canonical: bool = False) -> None:
   184	        self._records: list[RunEvent | JournalEntry] = []
   185	        self._path = Path(path) if path else None
   186	        self._canonical = canonical
   187	        self._run_id: Optional[str] = None
   188	        self._snapshot_digest: Optional[str] = None
   189	        self._lock_fd: Optional[int] = None
   190	
   191	    @property
   192	    def is_canonical(self) -> bool:
   193	        return self._canonical
   194	
   195	    def initialize(
   196	        self, run_id: str, payload: dict[str, Any], *, snapshot_digest: str
   197	    ) -> RunEvent:
   198	        """Create canonical seq-0 ``run.started`` and bind stream identity."""
   199	        if not self._canonical:
   200	            raise ValueError("initialize is only valid for canonical journals")
   201	        if self._records:
   202	            raise ValueError("journal is already initialized")
   203	        return self.append_event(
   204	            "run.started", run_id, payload=payload, snapshot_digest=snapshot_digest
   205	        )
   206	
   207	    def append_event(
   208	        self,
   209	        kind: str,
   210	        run_id: str,
   211	        step_id: Optional[str] = None,
   212	        payload: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
   213	        *,
   214	        snapshot_digest: Optional[str] = None,
   215	        attempt_id: Optional[str] = None,
   216	    ) -> RunEvent | JournalEntry | None:
   217	        if not self._canonical:
   218	            # A resumed historical stream stays historical; never mix formats.
   219	            # Events with no old equivalent are intentionally absent there.
   220	            projected_kind: Optional[str]
   221	            projected_payload = dict(payload or {})
   222	            if kind in {"run.started", "step.started"}:
   223	                projected_kind = kind
   224	            elif kind == "verification.completed":
   225	                projected_kind = "step.attempt"
   226	            elif kind == "approval.required":
   227	                projected_kind = "hitl.requested"
   228	            elif kind == "approval.resolved":
   229	                projected_kind = "hitl.resolved"
   230	            elif kind in {"step.completed", "step.failed", "step.skipped"}:
   231	                projected_kind = kind
   232	            elif kind in {"run.completed", "run.failed"}:
   233	                projected_kind = "run.finished"
   234	                projected_payload.setdefault(
   235	                    "status", "completed" if kind == "run.completed" else "failed"
   236	                )
   237	            else:
   238	                projected_kind = None
   239	            if projected_kind is None:
   240	                return None
   241	            return self.append(
   242	                projected_kind, run_id, step_id=step_id, payload=projected_payload
   243	            )
   244	        with self.transaction(refresh=self._lock_fd is None):
   245	            digest = snapshot_digest or self._snapshot_digest
   246	            if digest is None:
   247	                raise ValueError("canonical events require a snapshot digest")
   248	            if self._run_id is not None and run_id != self._run_id:
   249	                raise ValueError(
   250	                    f"journal is bound to run {self._run_id!r}, not {run_id!r}"
   251	                )
   252	            if self._snapshot_digest is not None and digest != self._snapshot_digest:
   253	                raise ValueError("snapshot digest changed within journal")
   254	            event = RunEvent(
   255	                seq=len(self._records), at=time.time(), kind=kind,
   256	                run_id=run_id, snapshot_digest=digest, step_id=step_id,
   257	                attempt_id=attempt_id, payload=payload or {},
   258	            )
   259	            if event.seq == 0 and event.kind != "run.started":
   260	                raise ValueError("canonical journal must begin with run.started")

   465	                # A timeout gets one same-tier retry before escalation. This
   466	                # branch intentionally precedes ε-exploration handling: timeout
   467	                # FAILs are not banked in the matrix, so the exploration rule's
   468	                # "failure evidence" rationale does not apply. After the retry
   469	                # is consumed, another timeout escalates for progress/cost
   470	                # control even if that second route happened to be exploratory.
   471	                if task.worker_id:
   472	                    # A hard pin is an execution contract, not a routing hint:
   473	                    # every retry stays on that exact eligible identity. Never
   474	                    # exclude its tier or substitute an unrelated higher pool.
   475	                    if timeout_failure and n < task.max_attempts:

   477	                            "task_id": task.id,
   478	                            "after_attempt": n,

   482	                        })
   483	                elif timeout_failure:
   484	                    if decision.tier not in timeout_retry_used:
   485	                        timeout_retry_used.add(decision.tier)
   486	                        if n < task.max_attempts:
   487	                            forced_retry_tier = decision.tier
   488	                            self._record("task.timeout_retry", {
   489	                                "task_id": task.id,
   490	                                "after_attempt": n,
   491	                                "tier": decision.tier.value,

   493	                            })

   496	                        if next_tier is not None:
   497	                            excluded_tiers.add(decision.tier)
   498	                            outcome.escalations += 1
   499	
   500	                # an ε-explored failure is the benched member's, not the tier's:
   501	                # the FAIL is already banked in the matrix, so retrying lets the
   502	                # next decide() pick the best member on merit — escalating would
   503	                # pay a higher tier for evidence we chose to buy cheap
   504	                elif not decision.explored:
   505	                    next_tier = self.router.next_tier(decision.tier)
   506	                    if next_tier is not None:
   507	                        excluded_tiers.add(decision.tier)
   508	                        outcome.escalations += 1

   541	    def _verification_event(
   542	        n: int, result: WorkerResult, verification: VerificationResult
   543	    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
   544	        """Stable run-event payload shared by live and legacy projections."""
   545	        return {
   546	            "n": n,
   547	            "worker_id": result.worker_id,
   548	            "model": result.model,
   549	            "tier": result.tier.value,
   550	            "verdict": verification.verdict.value,

   552	            "detail": verification.detail[:300],

   554	                verification.failure_mode.value
   555	                if verification.failure_mode else None
   556	            ),
   557	            "latency_s": round(result.latency_s, 2),
   558	            "verification_latency_s": round(verification.latency_s, 2),
   559	            "timed_out": result.timed_out,
   560	        }
   420	                    )
   421	                except ValueError as exc:
   422	                    # a bad input reference must FAIL the run visibly — a stuck
   423	                    # "running" state with no journal trail is the worst outcome
   424	                    state.status = RunStatus.FAILED

   426	                    journal.append_event("step.failed", run_id, step_id=step.id,

   194	def test_context_manifest_is_a_canonical_attempt_scoped_kind(tmp_path):
   195	    """META-19 (F1): context.manifest is journaled as a canonical kind with an
   196	    attempt id; a durable Journal.load() round-trips it, and it has no legacy
   197	    projection (entries() must skip it, never crash)."""
   198	    from metaharness.workflows.journal import CANONICAL_KINDS
   199	
   200	    assert "context.manifest" in CANONICAL_KINDS
   201	    path = tmp_path / "manifest_run.jsonl"
   202	    journal = Journal(path=path, canonical=True)
   203	    journal.initialize("run_m", {"context": {}}, snapshot_digest="a" * 64)
   204	    journal.append_event("step.started", "run_m", step_id="work", payload={"task_id": "t1"})
   205	    event = journal.append_event(
   206	        "context.manifest", "run_m", step_id="work",
   207	        payload={"schema_version": 1, "shadow": False, "task_id": "t1", "round": 0, "n": 1},
   208	        attempt_id="work-attempt-1",
   209	    )
   210	    assert event.kind == "context.manifest"
   211	    assert event.attempt_id == "work-attempt-1"
   212	
   213	    reloaded = Journal.load(path)
   214	    manifests = [e for e in reloaded.events() if e.kind == "context.manifest"]
   215	    assert len(manifests) == 1
   216	    assert manifests[0].payload["shadow"] is False
   217	    # no legacy projection — the historical entries() view skips it silently
   218	    assert all(entry.kind != "context.manifest" for entry in reloaded.entries())
   219

   221	async def test_context_manifest_journaled_per_round_end_to_end(tmp_path):
   222	    """META-19 (test 4): a real run — engine -> executor -> worker ->
   223	    Journal.load() — journals one NON-shadow context.manifest per tool round,
   224	    each pinning the exact bytes that round sent, under the attempt id. No
   225	    context.manifest.shadow event exists anymore."""
   226	    import httpx
   227	
   228	    from metaharness.context import content_hash
   229	    from metaharness.harness import OpenAICompatWorker
   230	
   231	    sent: list[list[dict]] = []
   232	
   233	    class Client:
   234	        async def post(self, url, json=None, headers=None):
   235	            sent.append(json["messages"])
   236	            if len(sent) == 1:
   237	                message = {"content": None, "tool_calls": [
   238	                    {"id": "c1", "function": {"name": "probe", "arguments": "{}"}}]}
   239	            else:
   240	                message = {"content": "ok"}
   241	            return httpx.Response(
   242	                200, json={"choices": [{"message": message}]},
   243	                request=httpx.Request("POST", url),
   244	            )
   245	
   246	    class Registry:
   247	        workspace_root = ""
   248	
   249	        def openai_schemas(self, names):
   250	            return [{"type": "function", "function": {"name": "probe", "parameters": {}}}]
   251	
   252	        async def call(self, name, arguments, focus=""):
   253	            return "tool observation"
   254	
   255	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker(
   256	        "worker-a", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="m",
   257	        client=Client(), tool_registry=Registry(),
   258	    )
   259	    executor = TaskExecutor(Router({Tier.SMALL: worker}))
   260	    spec = WorkflowSpec.model_validate({
   261	        "name": "tool-run",
   262	        "steps": [{"id": "work", "objective": "use probe", "tools": ["probe"],
   263	                   "success_check": {"equals": "ok"}}],
   264	    })
   265	    engine = WorkflowEngine(executor, journal_dir=tmp_path)
   266	    run = engine.start(spec)
   267	    run = await engine.advance(run.run_id)
   268	    assert run.status is RunStatus.COMPLETED
   269	
   270	    journal = Journal.load(tmp_path / f"{run.run_id}.jsonl")
   271	    manifests = [e for e in journal.events() if e.kind == "context.manifest"]
   272	    assert len(manifests) == 2
   273	    assert [e.payload["round"] for e in manifests] == [0, 1]
   274	    assert all(e.payload["shadow"] is False for e in manifests)
   275	    assert all(e.attempt_id == "work-attempt-1" for e in manifests)
   276	    for event, messages in zip(manifests, sent):
   277	        assert event.payload["live_messages_hash"] == content_hash(messages)
   278	    assert not any(e.kind == "context.manifest.shadow" for e in journal.events())
   279	    # the new kind has no legacy projection and never crashes entries()
   280	    assert all(entry.kind != "context.manifest" for entry in journal.entries())

   255	def test_shadow_manifest_records_tool_schemas_outside_live_message_reconstruction():

   262	        messages,

   273	async def test_local_worker_emits_live_manifest_and_divergence_is_impossible():
   274	    """META-19 (supersedes the shadow-manifest test): the worker consumes the
   275	    LIVE assembler, emits a NON-shadow context.manifest, and the manifest's
   276	    reconstruct_messages() equals the bytes the client actually received —
   277	    divergence between manifest and sent bytes is impossible by construction."""
   278	    seen = {}
   279	
   280	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   281	        seen["body"] = json.loads(request.content)
   282	        return httpx.Response(
   283	            200,
   284	            json={
   285	                "choices": [{"message": {"content": "done"}}],
   286	                "usage": {"prompt_tokens": 3, "completion_tokens": 1},
   287	            },
   288	        )
   289	
   290	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
   291	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker(
   292	        "local",
   293	        base_url="http://fake/v1",
   294	        model="m",
   295	        client=client,
   296	    )
   297	    task = Task(id="task-1", objective="do the exact task", boundaries=["stay bounded"])
   298	    events = []
   299	    token = bind_run_event_sink(lambda kind, payload: events.append((kind, payload)))
   300	    try:
   301	        result = await worker.run(task)
   302	    finally:
   303	        reset_run_event_sink(token)
   304	        await client.aclose()
   305	
   306	    assert result.output == "done"
   307	    expected_messages = [
   308	        {
   309	            "role": "system",
   310	            "content": "You are a worker agent executing one well-scoped task.\n\n"
   311	            "Boundaries:\n- stay bounded",
   312	        },
   313	        {"role": "user", "content": "do the exact task"},
   314	    ]
   315	    assert seen["body"]["messages"] == expected_messages
   316	    assert not any(kind == "context.manifest.shadow" for kind, _ in events)
   317	    live = [payload for kind, payload in events if kind == "context.manifest"]
   318	    assert len(live) == 1
   319	    assert live[0]["shadow"] is False
   320	    assert live[0]["round"] == 0
   321	    assert live[0]["manifest"]["model_id"] == "m"
   322	    assert live[0]["live_messages_hash"] == content_hash(seen["body"]["messages"])
   323	    persisted = ContextManifest.model_validate(live[0]["manifest"])
   324	    # divergence impossible: manifest reconstructs the exact sent bytes
   325	    assert persisted.reconstruct_messages() == seen["body"]["messages"]
   326

   328	async def test_local_worker_redacts_secret_from_sent_bytes():
   329	    """META-19 (test 2): a secret seeded into task inputs is [REDACTED] in the
   330	    bytes ACTUALLY sent to the endpoint (not just a shadow copy); the manifest's
   331	    redaction_count agrees, and the Authorization header keeps the real key."""
   332	    secret = "sk-live-super-secret-token-value"
   333	    seen = {}
   334	
   335	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   336	        seen["body"] = json.loads(request.content)
   337	        seen["auth"] = request.headers.get("Authorization")
   338	        return httpx.Response(200, json={"choices": [{"message": {"content": "done"}}]})
   339	
   340	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
   341	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker(
   342	        "local", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="m", api_key=secret, client=client,
   343	    )
   344	    task = Task(objective="use the credential", inputs={"token": secret})
   345	    events = []
   346	    token = bind_run_event_sink(lambda kind, payload: events.append((kind, payload)))
   347	    try:
   348	        await worker.run(task)
   349	    finally:
   350	        reset_run_event_sink(token)
   351	        await client.aclose()
   352	
   353	    body_text = json.dumps(seen["body"]["messages"])
   354	    assert secret not in body_text
   355	    assert "[REDACTED]" in body_text
   356	    assert seen["auth"] == f"Bearer {secret}"  # transport keeps the real key
   357	    live = [payload for kind, payload in events if kind == "context.manifest"][0]
   358	    assert live["manifest"]["redaction_count"] >= 1

   379	async def test_local_trust_violation_makes_no_model_call(monkeypatch):
   380	    """META-19 (test 1): a trust violation on the worker path raises before the
   381	    endpoint is ever hit; the runner tags error_kind='context_contract'."""
   382	    from metaharness.harness import local as local_mod
   383	
   384	    calls = {"n": 0}
   385	
   386	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   387	        calls["n"] += 1
   388	        return httpx.Response(200, json={"choices": [{"message": {"content": "x"}}]})
   389	
   390	    def bad_drafts(task, system_prompt=""):
   391	        return [SectionDraft(
   392	            section_type=ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   393	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   394	            stable_id="evil",
   395	            trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   396	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   397	            content="untrusted content masquerading as instructions",
   398	            role="system",
   399	        )]
   400	
   401	    monkeypatch.setattr(local_mod, "_build_drafts", bad_drafts)
   402	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
   403	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker("local", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="m", client=client)
   404	    try:
   405	        result = await worker.run(Task(objective="x"))
   406	    finally:
   407	        await client.aclose()
   408	
   409	    assert calls["n"] == 0  # fail closed: endpoint NEVER hit
   410	    assert result.error_kind == "context_contract"
   411	    assert "LiveContextViolation" in (result.error or "")

   414	def test_assemble_live_is_deterministic():
   415	    """META-19 (test 6): identical inputs -> identical envelope/manifest hashes."""
   416	    drafts = [
   417	        SectionDraft(

   438	async def test_manifest_sink_failure_cannot_change_worker_execution():
   439	    """META-19 (retained): a telemetry sink is outside candidate execution
   440	    authority — a failing context.manifest emit must NOT fail the model call.
   441	    Only the legacy-fallback-on-assembler-error assertion is superseded."""
   442	    seen = {}
   443	
   444	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   445	        seen["body"] = json.loads(request.content)
   446	        return httpx.Response(200, json={"choices": [{"message": {"content": "done"}}]})
   447	
   448	    def broken_sink(kind, payload):
   449	        if kind == "context.manifest":
   450	            raise RuntimeError("journal unavailable")
   451	
   452	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
   453	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker("local", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="m", client=client)
   454	    token = bind_run_event_sink(broken_sink)
   455	    try:
   456	        result = await worker.run(Task(objective="still run"))
   457	    finally:
   458	        reset_run_event_sink(token)
   459	        await client.aclose()
   460	
   461	    assert result.output == "done"
   462	    assert seen["body"]["messages"][-1]["content"] == "still run"

   465	async def test_assembler_failure_fails_closed_with_no_model_call(monkeypatch):
   466	    """META-19 (SUPERSEDES test_shadow_assembler_failure_falls_back_to_legacy_fit):
   467	    the legacy fallback is REMOVED. A LiveContextViolation propagates — no model
   468	    call, no shadow_failed event — and surfaces as error_kind='context_contract'."""
   469	    calls = {"n": 0}
   470	
   471	    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
   472	        calls["n"] += 1
   473	        return httpx.Response(200, json={"choices": [{"message": {"content": "done"}}]})
   474	
   475	    def fail_assembly(*args, **kwargs):
   476	        raise LiveContextViolation("contract breach")
   477	
   478	    # assemble_live is imported lazily inside _execute (import-cycle avoidance),
   479	    # so patch it on the context package where the name is looked up at call time.
   480	    monkeypatch.setattr("metaharness.context.assemble_live", fail_assembly)
   481	    events = []
   482	    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
   483	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker("local", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="m", client=client)
   484	    token = bind_run_event_sink(lambda kind, payload: events.append((kind, payload)))
   485	    try:
   486	        result = await worker.run(Task(objective="fail closed"))
   487	    finally:
   488	        reset_run_event_sink(token)
   489	        await client.aclose()
   490	
   491	    assert calls["n"] == 0  # fail closed: no model call
   492	    assert result.error_kind == "context_contract"
   493	    assert not any(kind.startswith("context.manifest") for kind, _ in events)

   496	async def test_second_tool_round_keeps_tool_observation_untrusted():
   497	    class Registry:
   498	        workspace_root = ""
   499	
   500	        def openai_schemas(self, names):
   501	            return [{"type": "function", "function": {"name": "probe", "parameters": {}}}]
   502	
   503	        async def call(self, name, arguments, focus=""):
   504	            return "untrusted tool observation"
   505	
   506	    class Client:
   507	        def __init__(self):
   508	            self.calls = 0
   509	
   510	        async def post(self, url, json=None, headers=None):
   511	            self.calls += 1
   512	            if self.calls == 1:
   513	                message = {
   514	                    "content": None,
   515	                    "tool_calls": [{
   516	                        "id": "call-1",
   517	                        "function": {"name": "probe", "arguments": "{}"},
   518	                    }],
   519	                }
   520	            else:
   521	                message = {"content": "done"}
   522	            return httpx.Response(
   523	                200,
   524	                json={"choices": [{"message": message}]},
   525	                request=httpx.Request("POST", url),
   526	            )
   527	
   528	    events = []
   529	    sent = []
   530	
   531	    client = Client()
   532	    _orig_post = client.post
   533	
   534	    async def _record_post(url, json=None, headers=None):
   535	        sent.append(json["messages"])
   536	        return await _orig_post(url, json=json, headers=headers)
   537	
   538	    client.post = _record_post
   539	    worker = OpenAICompatWorker(
   540	        "local",
   541	        base_url="http://fake/v1",
   542	        model="m",
   543	        client=client,
   544	        tool_registry=Registry(),
   545	    )
   546	    token = bind_run_event_sink(lambda kind, payload: events.append((kind, payload)))
   547	    try:
   548	        result = await worker.run(Task(objective="use probe", tools=["probe"]))
   549	    finally:
   550	        reset_run_event_sink(token)
   551	
   552	    assert result.output == "done"
   553	    # META-19 (supersedes shadow tool-round test): live, non-shadow manifests,
   554	    # one per round, each reconstructing the exact bytes that round sent.
   555	    assert not any(kind == "context.manifest.shadow" for kind, _ in events)
   556	    payloads = [payload for kind, payload in events if kind == "context.manifest"]
   557	    manifests = [ContextManifest.model_validate(p["manifest"]) for p in payloads]
   558	    assert len(manifests) == 2
   559	    assert [p["round"] for p in payloads] == [0, 1]
   560	    for payload, messages in zip(payloads, sent):
   561	        assert payload["live_messages_hash"] == content_hash(messages)
   562	    second_messages = manifests[1].reconstruct_messages()
   563	    assert second_messages == sent[1]  # divergence impossible in round 2
   564	    tool_index = next(index for index, message in enumerate(second_messages) if message["role"] == "tool")
   565	    tool_entry = [entry for entry in manifests[1].entries if entry.surface == "message"][tool_index]
   566	    assert tool_entry.trust == ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE
   567	    assert tool_entry.source_kind == ContextSourceKind.IMMUTABLE_ARTIFACT
   430

   432	# -- META-19: live context assembler on the coding path -----------------------
   433	
   434	
   435	@pytest.mark.parametrize("cli,sends_system", [
   436	    ("pi", True), ("codex", False), ("opencode", False), ("claude", True),
   437	])
   438	async def test_coding_adapters_emit_live_manifest_and_attest_system_prompt(
   439	    tmp_path, cli, sends_system,
   440	):
   441	    """META-19 (F8): all four CLI adapters consume the live assembler. The flat
   442	    prompt carries objective/constraints/inputs; the manifest is emitted once per
   443	    attempt (round 0); a system_prompt surface is attested ONLY for adapters that
   444	    actually transport one (pi/claude), and its redacted value reaches argv."""
   445	    ws = tmp_path / "ws"
   446	    binary = _capturing_stub(tmp_path, cli)
   447	    worker = CodingAgentWorker(
   448	        f"w-{cli}", cli=cli, workspace=ws, binary=binary,
   449	        system_prompt="PERSONA-MARKER",
   450	    )
   451	    task = _task(objective="fix the bug", boundaries=["do not touch tests"],
   452	                 inputs={"file": "a.py", "_hidden": "nope"})
   453	    result, events = await _run_capturing(worker, task)
   454	
   455	    assert result.error is None
   456	    assert result.output == "done"
   457	    manifests = [p for k, p in events if k == "context.manifest"]
   458	    assert not any(k == "context.manifest.shadow" for k, _ in events)
   459	    assert len(manifests) == 1
   460	    assert manifests[0]["shadow"] is False and manifests[0]["round"] == 0
   461	    manifest = ContextManifest.model_validate(manifests[0]["manifest"])
   462	    surfaces = {entry.surface for entry in manifest.entries}
   463	    assert "flat_prompt" in surfaces
   464	    assert ("system_prompt" in surfaces) is sends_system
   465	
   466	    flat = next(json.loads(e.payload_json) for e in manifest.entries
   467	                if e.surface == "flat_prompt")
   468	    assert "fix the bug" in flat
   469	    assert "do not touch tests" in flat
   470	    assert "a.py" in flat and "nope" not in flat
   471	    assert "PERSONA-MARKER" not in flat  # system prompt is a distinct surface
   472	
   473	    argv = (ws / "argv.txt").read_text()
   474	    if sends_system:
   475	        assert "--append-system-prompt" in argv and "PERSONA-MARKER" in argv
   476	    else:
   477	        assert "PERSONA-MARKER" not in argv  # truthful: adapter transports none

   517	async def test_coding_trust_violation_makes_no_cli_call(tmp_path, monkeypatch):
   518	    """META-19 (test 1, coding): a trust violation fails closed — the CLI binary
   519	    is never spawned — and surfaces as error_kind='context_contract'."""
   520	    from metaharness.context import (
   521	        ContextSectionType, ContextSourceKind, ContextTrust, SectionDraft, Sensitivity,
   522	    )
   523	    from metaharness.harness import coding as coding_mod
   524	
   525	    ws = tmp_path / "ws"
   526	    marker = ws / "spawned"
   527	    binary = _stub(tmp_path, "codex", f'touch "{marker}"; echo done')
   528	
   529	    def bad_drafts(task, *, system_prompt):
   530	        return [SectionDraft(
   531	            section_type=ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   532	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   533	            stable_id="evil", trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   534	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL, content="untrusted", role="user",
   535	        )]
   536	
   537	    monkeypatch.setattr(coding_mod, "_build_drafts", bad_drafts)
   538	    worker = CodingAgentWorker("cx", cli="codex", workspace=ws, binary=binary)
   539	    result = await worker.run(_task(objective="x"))
   540	    assert result.error_kind == "context_contract"
   640	    failure as budget exhaustion. A worker that errors AND blows the cap on the
   641	    same attempt must record the real TOOL_ERROR — the run still stops (budget
   642	    event recorded), it just doesn't lie about why."""
   643	    from metaharness.core.types import MASTMode
   644	
   645	    class Failing(Runner):
   646	        worker_id, tier, model = "w", Tier.SMALL, "w"
   647	        async def run(self, task):
   648	            return WorkerResult(task_id=task.id, worker_id="w", tier=self.tier,
   649	                                model="w", error="tool blew up",
   650	                                tokens_in=30, tokens_out=10)
   651	
   652	    budget = Budget(max_tokens=5)  # the 40-token charge blows the cap
   653	    executor = TaskExecutor(Router({Tier.SMALL: Failing()}), budget=budget)
   654	    outcome = await executor.execute(classify_task(max_attempts=3))
   655	    assert outcome.final_verdict == Verdict.FAIL
   656	    assert len(outcome.attempts) == 1  # the budget stop still halts the run
   657	    assert outcome.attempts[-1].verification.failure_mode == MASTMode.TOOL_ERROR
   658	    assert outcome.attempts[-1].verification.scorer == "execution"
   659	    assert budget.spent_tokens == 40  # charged regardless
   660

   672	async def test_reflection_feeds_next_attempt():
   673	    # META-19 (F2): reflections now accumulate in task.advice, not boundaries.
   674	    # Advice quotes prior worker output verbatim; keeping it out of the
   675	    # caller-authored boundaries contract prevents untrusted-data laundering.
   676	    seen_advice: list[list[str]] = []
   677	    seen_boundaries: list[list[str]] = []
   678	
   679	    def handler(task: Task):
   680	        seen_advice.append(list(task.advice))
   681	        seen_boundaries.append(list(task.boundaries))
   682	        return "negative"  # always wrong
   683	
   684	    runner = ScriptedWorker("w", handler)
   685	    executor = TaskExecutor(
   686	        Router({Tier.SMALL: runner}),
   687	        reflector=lambda task, attempt: f"attempt {attempt.n} returned {attempt.result.output!r}; that is wrong",
   688	    )
   689	    await executor.execute(classify_task(max_attempts=3))
   690	    assert seen_advice[0] == []
   691	    assert any("wrong" in b for b in seen_advice[1])
   692	    # repetition notice also appears once the same wrong answer recurs
   693	    assert any("different approach" in b.lower() for b in seen_advice[2])
   694	    # boundaries stay the pure caller-authored contract across every attempt
   695	    assert all(b == seen_boundaries[0] for b in seen_boundaries)
   696
