   698	async def test_provenance_trail_written_and_verifiable():
   699	    orch_kp = KeyPair.generate()
   700	    registry = WorkerRegistry()
   701	    register(registry, "orchestrator", orch_kp)
   702	    provenance = ProvenanceLog()
   703	    runner = MockLLMWorker("w", Tier.SMALL, seed=1, skills={TaskType.CLASSIFY: 1.0})
   704	    executor = TaskExecutor(
   705	        Router({Tier.SMALL: runner}),
   706	        provenance=provenance,
   707	        orchestrator_keypair=orch_kp,
   708	    )
   709	    await executor.execute(classify_task())
   710	    kinds = [e.action for e in provenance.entries()]
   711	    assert kinds[0] == "task.started" and kinds[-1] == "task.finished"
   712	    assert "task.attempt" in kinds
   713	    check = provenance.verify_chain(
   714	        lambda wid: registry.get(wid).public_key_b64 if registry.get(wid) else None
   715	    )
   716	    assert check.ok, check.reason

   719	async def test_observer_receives_every_outcome():
   720	    """Regression (2026-07-08): LearningLoop.observe was never wired into the
   721	    server path, so WebUI failure clusters stayed empty forever. The executor
   722	    now notifies an observer for each finished task."""

   730	                            playbook_hints=loop.hints_for, observer=loop.observe)

   732	    assert loop.stats.count("classify", MASTMode.DISOBEY_TASK_SPEC) >= 1

    63	        ContextSectionType.WORKFLOW_STATE: 10,
    64	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS: 18,
    65	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY: 11,
    66	        ContextSectionType.POPULATION_FINDINGS: 7,
    67	        ContextSectionType.VERIFIER_FEEDBACK: 6,
    68	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT: 4,
    69	    },
    70	}
    71	
    72	
    73	def estimate_tokens(text: str) -> int:
    74	    return len(text) // 4 + 1
    75	
    76	
    77	def messages_tokens(messages: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> int:
    78	    return sum(estimate_tokens(str(message.get("content") or "")) for message in messages)
    79	
    80	
    81	def budget_for(tier: Tier, override: int | None = None) -> int:
    82	    budget = override or TIER_CONTEXT_BUDGET.get(tier, 8_000)
    83	    return int(budget * (1 - GENERATION_RESERVE))
    84	
    85	
    86	def allocate_section_budgets(
    87	    section_types: list[ContextSectionType],
    88	    budget_tokens: int,
    89	    tier: Tier,
    90	) -> list[int]:
    91	    """Allocate the whole budget by tier using deterministic largest remainder."""
    92	    if budget_tokens < 0:
    93	        raise ValueError("budget_tokens must be nonnegative")
    94	    if not section_types:
    95	        return []
    96	    weights = TIER_SECTION_WEIGHTS[tier]
    97	    raw_weights = [weights[section_type] for section_type in section_types]
    98	    total_weight = sum(raw_weights)
    99	    numerators = [budget_tokens * weight for weight in raw_weights]
   100	    allocations = [numerator // total_weight for numerator in numerators]
   101	    remaining = budget_tokens - sum(allocations)
   102	    order = sorted(
   103	        range(len(section_types)),
   104	        key=lambda index: (-(numerators[index] % total_weight), index),
   105	    )
   106	    for index in order[:remaining]:
   107	        allocations[index] += 1
   108	    return allocations
   109	
   110	
   111	def fit_messages(messages: list[dict[str, Any]], budget_tokens: int) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   112	    """Preserve the pre-contract fitting behavior exactly for existing callers."""
   113	    if messages_tokens(messages) <= budget_tokens:
   114	        return messages
   115	    result = [dict(message) for message in messages]
   116	    prunable = [
   117	        index
   118	        for index, message in enumerate(result)
   119	        if not (index == 0 and message.get("role") == "system")
   120	        and index != len(result) - 1
   121	    ]
   122	
   123	    def priority(index: int) -> tuple[int, int]:
   124	        role_rank = 0 if result[index].get("role") == "tool" else 1
   125	        return role_rank, -len(str(result[index].get("content") or ""))
   126	
   127	    for index in sorted(prunable, key=priority):
   128	        if messages_tokens(result) <= budget_tokens:
   129	            break
   130	        text = str(result[index].get("content") or "")
   131	        overshoot = messages_tokens(result) - budget_tokens
   132	        target_chars = max(400, len(text) - overshoot * 4 - 200)
   133	        if target_chars < len(text):
   134	            result[index]["content"] = digest_text(text, target_chars)
   135	    return result
   136	
   137	
   138	class ContextFitReceipt(BaseModel):
   139	    """Internal sidecar: live messages plus the safe durable shadow receipt."""
   140	
   141	    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid", frozen=True)
   142	    messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   143	    redacted_messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   144	    envelope: ContextEnvelope
   145	    manifest: ContextManifest
   146	
   147	
   148	_BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS = (
   149	    re.compile(r"\bsk-[A-Za-z0-9_-]{8,}\b"),
   150	    re.compile(r"(?i)(authorization\s*:\s*bearer\s+)[^\s,;]+"),
   151	)
   152	
   153	
   154	def _redact_string(value: str, redaction_values: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[str, int]:
   155	    redacted = value
   156	    count = 0
   157	    for secret in redaction_values:
   158	        occurrences = redacted.count(secret)
   159	        if occurrences:
   160	            redacted = redacted.replace(secret, "[REDACTED]")
   161	            count += occurrences
   162	    for pattern in _BUILTIN_SECRET_PATTERNS:
   163	        def replace(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
   164	            nonlocal count
   165	            count += 1
   166	            prefix = match.group(1) if match.lastindex else ""
   167	            return prefix + "[REDACTED]"
   168	
   169	        redacted = pattern.sub(replace, redacted)
   170	    return redacted, count
   171	
   172	
   173	def _redact(value: Any, redaction_values: tuple[str, ...]) -> tuple[Any, int]:
   174	    if isinstance(value, str):
   175	        return _redact_string(value, redaction_values)
   176	    if isinstance(value, list):
   177	        output, total = [], 0
   178	        for item in value:
   179	            clean, count = _redact(item, redaction_values)
   180	            output.append(clean)
   181	            total += count
   182	        return output, total
   183	    if isinstance(value, dict):
   184	        output, total = {}, 0
   185	        for key in sorted(value):
   186	            clean_key, key_count = _redact_string(key, redaction_values)
   187	            if clean_key != key:
   188	                clean_key = f"[REDACTED_KEY_{len(output)}]"
   189	            clean, count = _redact(value[key], redaction_values)
   190	            output[clean_key] = clean
   191	            total += key_count + count
   192	        return output, total
   193	    return value, 0
   194	
   195	
   196	def _message_contract(index: int, total: int, role: str) -> tuple[ContextSectionType, ContextSourceKind, ContextTrust]:
   197	    if index == 0 and role == "system":
   198	        return (
   199	            ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   200	            ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
   201	            ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   202	        )
   203	    if role == "tool":
   204	        return (
   205	            ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   206	            ContextSourceKind.IMMUTABLE_ARTIFACT,
   207	            ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   208	        )
   209	    if role == "assistant":
   210	        return (
   211	            ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   212	            ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
   213	            ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
   214	        )
   215	    if index == total - 1:
   216	        return (
   217	            ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   218	            ContextSourceKind.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   219	            ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   220	        )
   221	    return ContextSectionType.TASK_CONTRACT, ContextSourceKind.GOAL, ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION
   222

    12	def _contains_traversal_segment(value: str) -> bool:
    13	    """A segment equal to '..' (forward or backslash separated) is path traversal."""
    14	    if not value:
    15	        return False
    16	    return ".." in value.replace("\\", "/").split("/")

    19	SHA256_PATTERN = r"^sha256:[0-9a-f]{64}$"

    21	
    22	def canonical_json(value: Any) -> str:
    23	    return json.dumps(value, ensure_ascii=False, sort_keys=True, separators=(",", ":"))
    24	
    25	
    26	def content_hash(value: Any) -> str:
    27	    material = value if isinstance(value, str) else canonical_json(value)
    28	    return "sha256:" + hashlib.sha256(material.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

    85	
    86	class ContextVersionBindings(FrozenModel):
    87	    """The immutable evidence/lineage tuple for one context assembly.
    88	
    89	    Cross-axis convention (documented): a `harness_version` self-declaring
    90	    a breaking schema change (a '-breaking-' segment in the version string)
    91	    must not bind a non-None `memory_snapshot_version` or
    92	    `evidence_snapshot_version`. Reusing those snapshots across a breaking
    93	    bump silently passes the per-axis checks today; the convention forces
    94	    callers to pick a fresh (or explicitly-None) snapshot pair, with a
    95	    future reconciliation marker providing the opt-in to reuse.
    96	    """
    97	
    98	    model_portfolio_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
    99	    harness_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   100	    evaluator_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   101	    weight_snapshot_version: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   102	    memory_snapshot_version: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   103	    evidence_snapshot_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   104	    candidate_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   105	    parent_candidate_version: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   106	
   107	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   108	    def validate_lineage(self) -> "ContextVersionBindings":
   109	        if self.parent_candidate_version == self.candidate_version:
   110	            raise ValueError("candidate and parent versions must differ")
   111	        if "breaking" in self.harness_version.split("-"):
   112	            if self.memory_snapshot_version is not None or self.evidence_snapshot_version is not None:
   113	                raise ValueError(
   114	                    "harness_version declares a breaking schema change "
   115	                    "('-breaking-' segment); memory_snapshot_version and "
   116	                    "evidence_snapshot_version must be None rather than "
   117	                    "reusing prior-version snapshots across the bump "
   118	                    "(future reconciliation marker: not yet supported)"
   119	                )
   120	        return self
   121	
   122	
   123	class ContextScope(FrozenModel):
   124	    project_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   125	    run_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   126	    task_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   127	    attempt_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   128	    lineage_id: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   129	
   130	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   131	    def validate_nesting(self) -> "ContextScope":
   132	        if self.task_id is not None and self.run_id is None:
   133	            raise ValueError("task_id requires run_id")
   134	        if self.attempt_id is not None and self.task_id is None:
   135	            raise ValueError("attempt_id requires task_id")
   136	        return self
   137	
   138	
   139	class ContextSourceRef(FrozenModel):
   140	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   141	    source_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   142	    kind: ContextSourceKind
   143	    scope: ContextScope
   144	    trust: ContextTrust
   145	    content_hash: str | None = Field(default=None, pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   146	    high_water_mark: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   147	    selection_reason: str = Field(min_length=1)
   148	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   149	    fetchable: bool
   150	    artifact_ref: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   151	
   152	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   153	    def validate_identity_and_fetch(self) -> "ContextSourceRef":
   154	        if (self.content_hash is None) == (self.high_water_mark is None):
   155	            raise ValueError("exactly one of content_hash or high_water_mark is required")
   156	        if self.fetchable != (self.artifact_ref is not None):
   157	            raise ValueError("fetchable sources require exactly one artifact_ref")
   158	        if _contains_traversal_segment(self.source_id):
   159	            raise ValueError(
   160	                "source_id must not contain path-traversal sequences "
   161	                "(e.g. '..' / '..\\..\\' segments)"
   162	            )
   163	        if self.artifact_ref is not None and _contains_traversal_segment(self.artifact_ref):
   164	            raise ValueError(
   165	                "artifact_ref must not contain path-traversal sequences "
   166	                "(e.g. '..' / '..\\..\\' segments)"
   167	            )
   168	        if (
   169	            self.kind is ContextSourceKind.EVALUATOR_RECEIPT
   170	            and self.trust is ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION
   171	        ):
   172	            raise ValueError(
   173	                "evaluator_receipt sources are evidence and may never "
   174	                "carry INSTRUCTION trust (no self-promotion to instruction "
   175	                "authority)"
   176	            )
   177	        return self
   178	
   179	
   180	class ContextSection(FrozenModel):
   181	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   182	    section_type: ContextSectionType
   183	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   184	    source: ContextSourceRef
   185	    source_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   186	    trust: ContextTrust
   187	    content: str
   188	    original_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   189	    selected_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   190	    compressed_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   191	    budget_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   192	    ordering_priority: int = Field(ge=0)
   193	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   194	    redaction_markers: tuple[str, ...] = ()
   195	    compression_action: CompressionAction = CompressionAction.NONE
   196	    omission_reason: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   197	    retrieval_score: float | None = None
   198	
   199	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   200	    def validate_provenance_and_counts(self) -> "ContextSection":
   201	        if self.source.content_hash is not None and self.source_hash != self.source.content_hash:
   202	            raise ValueError("source_hash must match source.content_hash")
   203	        if self.trust != self.source.trust:
   204	            raise ValueError("section trust must match source trust")
   205	        if self.sensitivity != self.source.sensitivity:
   206	            raise ValueError("section sensitivity must match source sensitivity")
   207	        if self.selected_tokens > self.original_tokens:
   208	            raise ValueError("selected token count cannot exceed original")
   209	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.NONE:
   210	            if self.omission_reason is not None:
   211	                raise ValueError("uncompressed sections cannot have an omission reason")
   212	            if self.compressed_tokens != self.selected_tokens:
   213	                raise ValueError("uncompressed token counts must match")
   214	        elif self.omission_reason is None:
   215	            raise ValueError("compression or omission requires a reason")
   216	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED and self.content:
   217	            raise ValueError("omitted sections cannot retain content")
   218	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED and self.compressed_tokens != 0:
   219	            raise ValueError("omitted sections must have zero rendered tokens")
   220	        if self.section_type in {
   221	            ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   222	            ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   223	        } and self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED:
   224	            raise ValueError("protected edge sections cannot be omitted")
   225	        return self
   226	
   227	
   228	class ContextEnvelope(FrozenModel):
   229	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   230	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   231	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   232	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   233	    sections: tuple[ContextSection, ...]
   234	    content_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   235	
   236	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   237	    def validate_hash_and_order(self) -> "ContextEnvelope":
   238	        if len({section.stable_id for section in self.sections}) != len(self.sections):
   239	            raise ValueError("section stable_id values must be unique")
   240	        priorities = [section.ordering_priority for section in self.sections]

   144	    def _tool_schemas(self, task: Task) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   145	        if not task.tools or self.tool_registry is None:
   146	            return []
   147	        return self.tool_registry.openai_schemas(task.tools)
   148	
   149	    def _body(self, task: Task, messages: list[dict[str, Any]],
   150	              tool_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   151	        body: dict[str, Any] = {
   152	            "model": self.model,
   153	            "messages": messages,
   154	            "temperature": self.temperature,
   155	        }
   156	        if self.max_tokens is not None:
   157	            body["max_tokens"] = self.max_tokens
   158	        if tool_schemas:
   159	            body["tools"] = tool_schemas
   160	        if task.output_schema:
   161	            body["response_format"] = {"type": "json_object"}
   162	        if self.thinking is not None:
   163	            body["chat_template_kwargs"] = {"enable_thinking": self.thinking}
   164	        body.update(self.extra_body)
   165	        return body

   167	    async def _post(self, client: httpx.AsyncClient, body: dict[str, Any],
   168	                    headers: dict[str, str]) -> dict[str, Any]:
   169	        resp = await client.post(
   170	            f"{self.base_url}/chat/completions", json=body, headers=headers
   171	        )
   172	        if resp.status_code == 400 and "response_format" in body:
   173	            # servers disagree on structured-output dialects (LM Studio wants
   174	            # json_schema, Ollama takes json_object) — the prompt already
   175	            # demands JSON, so retry bare rather than fail the attempt
   176	            body.pop("response_format")
   177	            resp = await client.post(
   178	                f"{self.base_url}/chat/completions", json=body, headers=headers
   179	            )
   180	        resp.raise_for_status()
   181	        return resp.json()

   217	                    # falls back to the exact legacy fitter.

   229	                            },

   267	
   268	def _dedupe(items: list[str]) -> list[str]:
   269	    seen: set[str] = set()
   270	    return [x for x in items if not (x in seen or seen.add(x))]

   272	
   273	def _render_prompt(task: Task) -> str:
   274	    """The Task delegation contract as one prompt for a coding agent."""
   275	    parts = [task.objective]
   276	    if task.boundaries:
   277	        parts.append("Constraints:\n" + "\n".join(f"- {b}" for b in task.boundaries))
   278	    visible = {k: v for k, v in (task.inputs or {}).items() if not k.startswith("_")}
   279	    if visible:
   280	        parts.append("Inputs:\n" + json.dumps(visible, ensure_ascii=False, default=str))
   281	    if task.output_schema:
   282	        parts.append(
   283	            "When done, print a final summary as a single JSON object matching:\n"
   284	            + json.dumps(task.output_schema)
   285	        )
   286	    return "\n\n".join(parts)

   288	
   289	class CodingAgentWorker(BaseRunner):
   290	    """A worker that runs a coding-agent CLI one-shot per task in a workspace.
   291	
   292	    Every run is headless and ephemeral (no CLI-side session state); the
   293	    workspace directory is the durable artifact. A non-zero exit or a spawn
   294	    failure becomes WorkerResult.error — loud, never a silent pass.
   295	    """
   296	
   297	    BASE_TIMEOUT_S: float = 600.0
   298	
   299	    def __init__(
   300	        self,
   301	        worker_id: str,
   302	        cli: str,
   303	        model: str = "",
   304	        tier: Tier = Tier.FRONTIER,
   305	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   306	        system_prompt: str = "",
   307	        workspace: Optional[Path] = None,   # default: per-task dir under ~/.metaharness/workspaces
   308	        binary: Optional[str] = None,       # override path (tests use a stub script)
   309	        extra_env: Optional[dict[str, str]] = None,
   310	        timeout_s: Optional[float] = None,  # None = task-type-aware default (issue #2)
   311	    ) -> None:
   312	        if cli not in CLI_ADAPTERS:
   313	            raise ValueError(f"unknown coding CLI '{cli}' (known: {sorted(CLI_ADAPTERS)})")
   314	        # model has two jobs kept strictly apart: `model` (display/matrix key,
   315	        # falls back to '<cli>-cli') vs `cli_model` (the explicit override the
   316	        # CLI receives; empty = the CLI's own configured default — a display
   317	        # placeholder must NEVER reach the command line)
   318	        super().__init__(worker_id=worker_id, tier=tier,
   319	                         model=model or f"{cli}-cli", keypair=keypair)
   320	        self.cli_model = model
   321	        self.cli = cli
   322	        self.adapter = CLI_ADAPTERS[cli]
   323	        self.system_prompt = system_prompt
   324	        self.workspace = Path(workspace) if workspace else None
   325	        self.binary = binary or self.adapter.binary
   326	        self.extra_env = extra_env or {}
   327	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s  # configured override; None = unset
   328	
   329	    def effective_timeout_s(self, task: Task) -> float:
   330	        """The timeout actually applied for one task: an explicit config
   331	        override wins flat across all task types; otherwise CODE_EDIT work
   332	        (a coding CLI implementing a plan) gets more room than a quick
   333	        one-shot text task (issue #2)."""
   334	        if self.timeout_s is not None:
   335	            return self.timeout_s
   336	        return self.BASE_TIMEOUT_S * TASK_TYPE_TIMEOUT_FACTOR.get(task.task_type, 1.0)
   337	
   338	    def _workspace_for(self, task: Task) -> Path:
   339	        explicit = (task.inputs or {}).get("_workspace")
   340	        ws = Path(explicit) if explicit else (
   341	            self.workspace or WORKSPACES_DIR / task.id
   342	        )
   343	        ws.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
   344	        return ws
   345	
   346	    async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   347	        workspace = self._workspace_for(task)
   348	        prompt = _render_prompt(task)
   349	        argv, stdin_text = self.adapter.build(self, prompt, workspace)
   350	        # Carry the full outer-host chain into nested harnesses. This blocks
   351	        # direct recursion and cycles such as Codex -> Pi -> Codex before spawn.
   352	        env = {
   353	            **os.environ,
   354	            **self.extra_env,
   355	            **child_host_environment(self.cli),
   356	        }
   357	
   358	        try:
   359	            proc = await asyncio.create_subprocess_exec(
   360	                *argv,
   361	                cwd=workspace,
   362	                env=env,
   363	                # Coding CLIs routinely spawn shells, tests, and helper agents.
   364	                # Give the attempt its own group so timeout/cancellation cannot
   365	                # leave descendants mutating the workspace after escalation.
   366	                start_new_session=True,
   367	                stdin=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE if stdin_text is not None else asyncio.subprocess.DEVNULL,
   368	                stdout=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   369	                stderr=asyncio.subprocess.PIPE,
   370	            )
   371	        except OSError as exc:
   372	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: cannot launch '{self.binary}': {exc}") from exc
   373	
   374	        eff = self.effective_timeout_s(task)
   375	        try:
   376	            stdout_b, stderr_b = await asyncio.wait_for(
   377	                proc.communicate(stdin_text.encode() if stdin_text is not None else None),
   378	                timeout=eff,
   379	            )
   380	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   381	            await self._terminate_process_group(proc)
   382	            # :g not :.0f — subsecond test timeouts (e.g. 0.5) must not render as "0s"
   383	            raise WorkerTimeout(f"{self.cli}: timed out after {eff:g}s", timeout_s=eff)
   384	        except asyncio.CancelledError:
   385	            await asyncio.shield(self._terminate_process_group(proc))
   386	            raise
   387	
   388	        stdout = stdout_b.decode(errors="replace")
   389	        stderr = stderr_b.decode(errors="replace")
   390	        if proc.returncode != 0:
   391	            detail = (stderr or stdout).strip()[-2000:]
   392	            raise RuntimeError(f"{self.cli}: exit {proc.returncode}: {detail}")
   393	
   394	        text, cost = self.adapter.parse(stdout)
   395	        from metaharness.harness.local import parse_output
   396	        # F3 (panel 2026-07-09, GLM P2): coding CLIs (codex/opencode) report cost
   397	        # 0.0 and no token usage, so CodeProposer charged ~nothing for the most
   398	        # expensive calls in the harness. No adapter surfaces a token count today,
   399	        # so ESTIMATE from character length (~4 chars/token) — a rough but non-zero
   400	        # figure so budget accounting reflects that these calls are not free.
   401	        tokens_in = len(prompt) // 4
   402	        tokens_out = len(text) // 4
   403	        return WorkerResult(
   404	            task_id=task.id,
   405	            worker_id=self.worker_id,
   406	            tier=self.tier,
   407	            model=self.model,
   408	            output=parse_output(text, expect_json=bool(task.output_schema)),
   409	            raw_text=text,
   410	            tokens_in=tokens_in,
   411	            tokens_out=tokens_out,
   412	            cost_usd=cost,
   413	            workspace_root=str(workspace),
   414	        )
   415	
   416	    @staticmethod
   417	    async def _terminate_process_group(proc: asyncio.subprocess.Process) -> None:
   418	        """Terminate and reap an attempt's complete POSIX process group."""
   419	        if proc.returncode is not None:
   420	            await proc.wait()
   421	            return
   422	        pgid = CodingAgentWorker._process_group_id(proc)
   423	        tracked = CodingAgentWorker._linux_descendant_pids(proc.pid)
   424	        CodingAgentWorker._signal_process_tree(proc, signal.SIGTERM, pgid, tracked)
   425	        try:
   426	            await asyncio.wait_for(proc.wait(), timeout=0.5)
   427	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   428	            pass
   429	        await asyncio.sleep(0.05)
   430	        tracked.update(CodingAgentWorker._linux_descendant_pids(proc.pid))
   431	        if (
   432	            proc.returncode is not None
   433	            and not CodingAgentWorker._group_alive(pgid)
   434	            and not CodingAgentWorker._any_pid_alive(tracked)
   435	        ):
   436	            return
   437	        CodingAgentWorker._signal_process_tree(proc, signal.SIGKILL, pgid, tracked)
   438	        try:
   439	            await asyncio.wait_for(proc.wait(), timeout=2.0)
   440	        except asyncio.TimeoutError:
   441	            if proc.returncode is None:
   442	                proc.kill()
   443	                await proc.wait()
   444	
   445	    @staticmethod
   446	    def _process_group_id(proc: asyncio.subprocess.Process) -> int | None:
   447	        try:
   448	            return os.getpgid(proc.pid)
   449	        except (ProcessLookupError, PermissionError, OSError):
   450	            return proc.pid
   451	
   452	    @staticmethod
   453	    def _group_alive(pgid: int | None) -> bool:
   454	        if pgid is None:
   455	            return False
   456	        try:
   457	            os.killpg(pgid, 0)
   458	            return True
   459	        except (ProcessLookupError, PermissionError, OSError):
   460	            return False
   461	
   462	    @staticmethod
   463	    def _pid_alive(pid: int) -> bool:
   464	        try:
   465	            os.kill(pid, 0)
   466	            return True
   467	        except (ProcessLookupError, PermissionError, OSError):
   468	            return False
   469	
   470	    @staticmethod

     async def execute(
         self, task: Task, *, event_sink: Optional[TaskEventSink] = None
     ) -> TaskOutcome:
         """Execute one task, optionally emitting live attempt/verification events.
 
         The callback is synchronous by design: the workflow journal fsyncs each
         event before execution moves past the corresponding transition.
         """
         def emit(kind: str, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
             if event_sink is not None:
                 event_sink(kind, payload)

 class Task(BaseModel):
     """A unit of work handed to a worker harness."""
 
     id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: _new_id("task"))
     task_type: TaskType = TaskType.GENERAL
     # explicit delegation contract (Anthropic multi-agent lesson): objective,
     # output format, and boundaries are load-bearing, not decoration.
     objective: str = ""
     inputs: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)

+    # META-19 (F2): accumulated reflections/knowledge hints, carried SEPARATELY
+    # from `boundaries`. Advice quotes prior worker output and retrieved content
+    # verbatim, so it is untrusted-derived and must never render into an
+    # instruction slot the way caller-authored boundaries do.
+    advice: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
     # a checkable success signal, if one exists. Interpreted by the verifier.
     success_check: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None
     tier_hint: Optional[Tier] = None
     # Human-friendly assignment constraints. ``worker_id`` is a hard pin;
     # role/capabilities are requirements that any selected worker must satisfy.
     role: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, exclude_if=lambda value: value is None)
     required_capabilities: list[str] = Field(
         default_factory=list, exclude_if=lambda value: not value
     )
     worker_id: Optional[str] = Field(default=None, exclude_if=lambda value: value is None)
     max_attempts: int = 3
     # tool names this task may call (small per-step subset, never the catalog)
     tools: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
     # Ask the orchestrator to attach a harness-owned, sandboxed test receipt.
     # This never grants the worker a command-execution tool.
     requires_execution_evidence: bool = False

 class WorkerResult(BaseModel):
     """What a worker harness returns for one attempt."""
 
     task_id: str
     worker_id: str
     tier: Tier
     model: str
     output: Any = None
     raw_text: str = ""
     tool_calls: list[dict[str, Any]] = Field(default_factory=list)
     tokens_in: int = 0
     tokens_out: int = 0
     cost_usd: float = 0.0
     latency_s: float = 0.0
     error: Optional[str] = None
+    # META-19 (F6): coarse classification of `error` for control flow. A
+    # deterministic context-contract violation ("context_contract") is not a
+    # model-capability signal — the executor aborts retries and excludes it from
+    # routing evidence. Other failures keep None (behavior unchanged).
+    error_kind: Optional[str] = None
     # Legacy v1 signatures covered only the worker's textual result. New v2
     # signatures also attest the execution-relevant metadata below. Keeping an
     # explicit version lets old journal signatures remain verifiable without
     # allowing their unsigned workspace_root to select code for execution.
     signature_version: int = 1
     # Derived metadata (issue #2): set by BaseRunner.run when `error` came from
     # a WorkerTimeout. It is covered by v2 signatures.
     timed_out: bool = False
     # the directory this worker's file side-effects land in (builtin tool jail
     # root or coding-CLI cwd), recorded by the runner that KNOWS it — evidence
     # collection and run packaging must never infer this from cwd or guess
     workspace_root: str = ""
     # detached signature over `result_signing_bytes(...)`, made with the worker's
     # registered key, so the orchestrator can confirm who produced this result.
     signature_b64: Optional[str] = None

     verdict: Verdict
     score: float = 0.0            # 0..1

    42	def _source(**changes):
    43	    values = {
    44	        "source_id": "repo-instructions",
    45	        "kind": ContextSourceKind.PROTECTED_INSTRUCTIONS,
    46	        "scope": ContextScope(project_id="meta-harness"),
    47	        "trust": ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
    48	        "content_hash": "sha256:" + "1" * 64,
    49	        "selection_reason": "required repository contract",
    50	        "sensitivity": Sensitivity.PUBLIC,
    51	        "fetchable": False,
    52	    }
    53	    values.update(changes)
    54	    return ContextSourceRef(**values)

    57	def _section(**changes):
    58	    source = changes.pop("source", _source())
    59	    values = {
    60	        "section_type": ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
    61	        "stable_id": "system-contract",

    66	        "original_tokens": 7,
    67	        "selected_tokens": 7,
    68	        "compressed_tokens": 7,
    69	        "budget_tokens": 100,
    70	        "ordering_priority": 0,
    71	        "sensitivity": source.sensitivity,
    72	        "compression_action": CompressionAction.NONE,
    73	    }
    74	    values.update(changes)
    75	    return ContextSection(**values)

   133	def test_tier_section_budgets_are_deterministic_complete_and_tier_specific():
   134	    sections = [
   135	        ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   136	        ContextSectionType.PRIOR_OUTPUTS,
   137	        ContextSectionType.MEMORY,
   138	        ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   139	    ]
   140	    small = allocate_section_budgets(sections, 1001, tier="small")
   141	    frontier = allocate_section_budgets(sections, 1001, tier="frontier")
   142	    assert small == allocate_section_budgets(sections, 1001, tier="small")
   143	    assert sum(small) == sum(frontier) == 1001
   144	    assert small != frontier
   145	    assert small[0] > frontier[0]
   146	    with pytest.raises(ValueError):
   147	        allocate_section_budgets(sections, -1, tier="small")

   150	def test_fit_receipt_is_deterministic_reconstructable_and_compatible():
   151	    messages = [
   152	        {"role": "system", "content": "contract " * 40},
   153	        {"role": "user", "content": "head-marker " + "middle " * 4000 + " tail-marker"},
   154	        {"role": "tool", "content": "tool-head " + "observation " * 4000 + " tool-tail"},
   155	        {"role": "user", "content": "final response contract"},
   156	    ]
   157	    original = copy.deepcopy(messages)
   158	
   159	    first = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   160	        messages,
   161	        budget_tokens=2600,
   162	        model_id="local-model",
   163	        harness_version="git:abc123",
   164	        policy_version="context-v1",
   165	    )
   166	    second = fit_messages_with_receipt(
   167	        copy.deepcopy(messages),
   168	        budget_tokens=2600,
   169	        model_id="local-model",
   170	        harness_version="git:abc123",
   171	        policy_version="context-v1",
   172	    )
   173	
   174	    assert messages == original
   175	    assert first.messages == fit_messages(messages, 2600)
   176	    assert first.model_dump_json() == second.model_dump_json()
   177	    assert first.manifest.reconstruct_messages() == first.redacted_messages
   178	    assert (
   179	        first.manifest.reconstruct_redacted_envelope().content_hash
   180	        == json.loads(first.manifest.redacted_envelope_json)["content_hash"]
   181	    )
   182	    assert first.envelope.content_hash == second.envelope.content_hash
   183	    assert first.manifest.manifest_hash == second.manifest.manifest_hash
   184	    assert first.messages[0] == messages[0]
   185	    assert first.messages[-1] == messages[-1]
   186	    compressed = [r for r in first.manifest.compression_receipts if r.action != "none"]
   187	    assert compressed
   188	    assert all(r.before_hash != r.after_hash for r in compressed)
   189	    assert "tool-head" in first.messages[2]["content"]
   190	    assert "tool-tail" in first.messages[2]["content"]

   323	    persisted = ContextManifest.model_validate(live[0]["manifest"])
   324	    # divergence impossible: manifest reconstructs the exact sent bytes
   325	    assert persisted.reconstruct_messages() == seen["body"]["messages"]

   330	    bytes ACTUALLY sent to the endpoint (not just a shadow copy); the manifest's

   439	    """META-19 (retained): a telemetry sink is outside candidate execution
   440	    authority — a failing context.manifest emit must NOT fail the model call.
   560	    for payload, messages in zip(payloads, sent):

   562	    second_messages = manifests[1].reconstruct_messages()

     1	"""Tool registry: one catalog of everything a worker may call — builtin tools
     2	and MCP-server tools — plus the selection logic that keeps per-step tool
     3	subsets SMALL.
     4	
     5	Design per memory/knowledge_base/context-engineering-agent-harnesses.md:
     6	- workers never see the full catalog: accuracy degrades with tool count, and
     7	  small local models degrade worst (RAG-MCP, MCPVerse). `select_for` returns
     8	  an adaptive shortlist (score cliff, cap 7).
     9	- schemas render deterministically (sorted keys, stable order) so a worker's
    10	  prompt prefix stays KV-cache-friendly across rounds.
    11	- tool RESULTS are pruned before they re-enter context: task-conditioned
    12	  digest with head/tail preserved (Squeez-style), never a silent truncation.
    13	"""
    14	from __future__ import annotations
    15	
    16	import inspect
    17	import hashlib
    18	import json
    19	import re
    20	from dataclasses import dataclass, field
    21	from typing import Any, Callable, Optional
    22	
    23	from metaharness.observability.run_events import emit_run_event
    24	
    25	MAX_RESULT_CHARS = 4_000
    26	DEFAULT_SUBSET_CAP = 7
    27	
    28	
    29	@dataclass
    30	class ToolSpec:
    31	    name: str
    32	    description: str
    33	    input_schema: dict[str, Any]                  # JSON schema for arguments
    34	    handler: Callable[..., Any]                   # sync or async; kwargs from args
    35	    source: str = "builtin"                       # builtin | mcp:<server>
    36	    keywords: tuple[str, ...] = ()                # extra terms for selection
    37	    annotations: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)  # MCP safety hints
    38	
    39	
    40	class ToolError(Exception):
    41	    """A tool failed; the message is worker-visible data, never instructions."""
    42	
    43	
    44	_WORD_RE = re.compile(r"[a-z0-9_]+")
    45	
    46	
    47	def _terms(text: str) -> set[str]:
    48	    return set(_WORD_RE.findall(text.lower()))
    49	
    50	
    51	def digest_text(text: str, max_chars: int = MAX_RESULT_CHARS,
    52	                focus_terms: Optional[set[str]] = None) -> str:
    53	    """Shrink a blob to budget, keeping focus-relevant lines plus head/tail.
    54	    The pruning is always LOUD — the reader sees exactly what was dropped."""
    55	    if len(text) <= max_chars:
    56	        return text
    57	    focus_terms = focus_terms or set()
    58	    kept: list[str] = []
    59	    used = 0
    60	    focus_budget = max_chars // 2
    61	    if focus_terms:
    62	        for line in text.splitlines():
    63	            if _terms(line) & focus_terms and used + len(line) < focus_budget:
    64	                kept.append(line)
    65	                used += len(line) + 1
    66	    remainder = max_chars - used
    67	    head = text[: int(remainder * 0.7)]
    68	    tail = text[-int(remainder * 0.3):] if remainder > 10 else ""
    69	    dropped = len(text) - used - len(head) - len(tail)
    70	    parts = [head, f"\n[…pruned {dropped} chars…]\n", tail]
    71	    if kept:
    72	        parts += ["\n[objective-relevant lines kept:]\n", "\n".join(kept)]
    73	    return "".join(parts)
    74	
    75	
    76	class ToolRegistry:
    77	    def __init__(self) -> None:
    78	        self._tools: dict[str, ToolSpec] = {}
    79	        # the jail root of this registry's file tools ("" = no file tools);
    80	        # workers stamp it onto WorkerResult.workspace_root so downstream
    81	        # consumers know where file side-effects actually landed
    82	        self.workspace_root: str = ""
    83	
    84	    def register(self, spec: ToolSpec) -> None:
    85	        if spec.name in self._tools:
    86	            raise ValueError(f"tool {spec.name!r} already registered")
    87	        self._tools[spec.name] = spec
    88	
    89	    def unregister_source(self, source: str) -> int:
    90	        """Drop every tool from one source (e.g. an MCP server being reloaded)."""
    91	        names = [n for n, t in self._tools.items() if t.source == source]
    92	        for name in names:
    93	            del self._tools[name]
    94	        return len(names)
    95	
    96	    def get(self, name: str) -> Optional[ToolSpec]:
    97	        return self._tools.get(name)
    98	
    99	    def all(self) -> list[ToolSpec]:
   100	        return [self._tools[n] for n in sorted(self._tools)]
   101	
   102	    def names(self) -> list[str]:
   103	        return sorted(self._tools)
   104	
   105	    # ------------------------------------------------------------- selection
   106	
   107	    def select_for(self, objective: str, boundaries: Optional[list[str]] = None,
   108	                   cap: int = DEFAULT_SUBSET_CAP) -> list[str]:
   109	        """Adaptive tool shortlist for one step: score by term overlap
   110	        (name 3x, keywords 2x, description 1x), keep tools above a cliff
   111	        relative to the best score, cap the subset. No signal -> NO tools;
   112	        most steps are pure text-work and tools would only confuse."""
   113	        text_terms = _terms(objective + " " + " ".join(boundaries or []))
   114	        scored: list[tuple[float, str]] = []
   115	        for name, tool in self._tools.items():
   116	            score = (
   117	                3.0 * len(text_terms & _terms(tool.name.replace(".", " ")))
   118	                + 2.0 * len(text_terms & _terms(" ".join(tool.keywords)))
   119	                + 1.0 * len(text_terms & _terms(tool.description))
   120	            )
   121	            if score > 0:
   122	                scored.append((score, name))
   123	        if not scored:
   124	            return []
   125	        scored.sort(key=lambda pair: (-pair[0], pair[1]))
   126	        top = scored[0][0]
   127	        cliff = max(2.0, 0.4 * top)
   128	        return [name for score, name in scored[:cap] if score >= cliff]
   129	
   130	    # -------------------------------------------------------------- schemas
   131	
   132	    def openai_schemas(self, names: list[str]) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   133	        """OpenAI function-calling schemas, deterministic order & serialization
   134	        (sorted by name; sorted keys downstream keeps the prefix byte-stable)."""
   135	        schemas = []
   136	        for name in sorted(set(names)):
   137	            tool = self._tools.get(name)
   138	            if tool is None:
   139	                continue  # a plan may reference a tool that has since unloaded
   140	            schemas.append({
   141	                "type": "function",
   142	                "function": {
   143	                    "name": tool.name.replace(".", "__"),  # dialect-safe name
   144	                    "description": tool.description,
   145	                    "parameters": tool.input_schema,
   146	                },
   147	            })
   148	        return schemas
   149	
   150	    def resolve_call_name(self, wire_name: str) -> Optional[str]:
   151	        """Map a dialect-safe wire name (dots escaped) back to the registry."""
   152	        if wire_name in self._tools:
   153	            return wire_name
   154	        dotted = wire_name.replace("__", ".")
   155	        return dotted if dotted in self._tools else None
   156	
   157	    # ------------------------------------------------------------ execution
   158	
   159	    async def call(self, name: str, arguments: dict[str, Any],
   160	                   focus: str = "") -> str:
   161	        """Run a tool; the return value is a pruned STRING (worker-facing).
   162	        Errors come back as data ('tool error: …') so the worker can adapt,
   163	        while a missing tool is a hard error — that's a harness bug."""
   164	        resolved = self.resolve_call_name(name)
   165	        if resolved is None:
   166	            raise ToolError(f"unknown tool {name!r}")
   167	        tool = self._tools[resolved]
   168	        # Stable, non-secret request identity: enough for approval/audit layers
   169	        # to correlate retries without copying argument values into journals.
   170	        request_bytes = json.dumps(
   171	            {"tool": resolved, "arguments": arguments}, sort_keys=True,
   172	            ensure_ascii=False, separators=(",", ":"), default=str,
   173	        ).encode("utf-8")
   174	        request_id = hashlib.sha256(request_bytes).hexdigest()
   175	        request_event = {
   176	            "tool": resolved,
   177	            "request_id": request_id,
   178	            "idempotency_key": request_id,
   179	            "argument_keys": sorted(str(key) for key in arguments),
   180	        }
   181	        emit_run_event("tool.requested", request_event)
   182	        try:
   183	            result = tool.handler(**arguments)
   184	            if inspect.isawaitable(result):
   185	                result = await result
   186	        except ToolError as exc:
   187	            result = f"tool error: {exc}"
   188	            emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "error"})
   189	            return result
   190	        except TypeError as exc:  # bad/missing arguments — worker can retry
   191	            result = f"tool error: bad arguments for {resolved}: {exc}"
   192	            emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "error"})
   193	            return result
   194	        except Exception:
   195	            emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "error"})
   196	            raise
   197	        if not isinstance(result, str):
   198	            result = json.dumps(result, ensure_ascii=False, default=str, sort_keys=True)
   199	        emit_run_event("tool.completed", {**request_event, "status": "completed"})
   200	        return digest_text(result, MAX_RESULT_CHARS, _terms(focus))

   276	    reason: str = Field(min_length=1)
   277	    fidelity_loss_estimate: float = Field(ge=0.0, le=1.0)
   278	
   279	    @model_validator(mode="before")
   280	    @classmethod
   281	    def _fill_fidelity_loss_estimate(cls, data: Any) -> Any:
   282	        if not isinstance(data, dict) or "fidelity_loss_estimate" in data:
   283	            return data
   284	        action = data.get("action")
   285	        original = data.get("original_tokens") or 0
   286	        final = data.get("final_tokens") or 0
   287	        if action is CompressionAction.NONE:
   288	            data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = 0.0
   289	            return data
   290	        if original <= 0:
   291	            data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = 0.0 if final <= 0 else 1.0
   292	            return data
   293	        loss = 1.0 - (final / original)
   294	        if loss < 0.0:
   295	            loss = 0.0
   296	        elif loss > 1.0:
   297	            loss = 1.0
   298	        data["fidelity_loss_estimate"] = loss
   299	        return data

   301	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   302	    def validate_change(self) -> "CompressionReceipt":
   303	        changed = self.before_hash != self.after_hash
   304	        if (self.action is CompressionAction.NONE) == changed:
   305	            raise ValueError("compression action must agree with before/after hashes")
   306	        return self

   309	class ContextManifestEntry(FrozenModel):
   310	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   311	    # META-19 (additive, F5): "flat_prompt" and "system_prompt" are the CLI
   312	    # transport surfaces the live assembler renders alongside chat messages.
   313	    # Additive only — existing "message"/"tool_schemas" semantics unchanged.
   314	    surface: Literal["message", "tool_schemas", "flat_prompt", "system_prompt"]
   315	    payload_json: str = Field(min_length=2)
   316	    source_kind: ContextSourceKind
   317	    trust: ContextTrust
   318	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   319	    source_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   320	    selected_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   321	    redacted: bool = False
   322	
   323	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   324	    def validate_payload(self) -> "ContextManifestEntry":
   325	        try:
   326	            payload = json.loads(self.payload_json)
   327	        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
   328	            raise ValueError("payload_json must be canonical JSON") from exc
   329	        if self.payload_json != canonical_json(payload):
   330	            raise ValueError("payload_json must be canonical JSON")
   331	        if self.surface == "message" and not isinstance(payload, dict):
   332	            raise ValueError("message payload must be an object")
   333	        if self.surface == "tool_schemas" and not (
   334	            isinstance(payload, list) and all(isinstance(item, dict) for item in payload)
   335	        ):
   336	            raise ValueError("tool_schemas payload must be an object array")
   337	        if self.selected_hash != content_hash(payload):
   338	            raise ValueError("selected_hash must attest payload_json")
   339	        return self
   340	
   341	
   342	class ContextManifest(FrozenModel):
   343	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   344	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   345	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   346	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   347	    envelope_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   348	    redacted_envelope_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   349	    redacted_envelope_json: str = Field(min_length=2)
   350	    entries: tuple[ContextManifestEntry, ...]
   351	    compression_receipts: tuple[CompressionReceipt, ...]
   352	    source_candidates_considered: tuple[str, ...]
   353	    visibility_decisions: tuple[str, ...]
   354	    deliberate_omissions: tuple[str, ...]
   355	    artifact_refs: tuple[str, ...]
   356	    budget_used_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   357	    budget_limit_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   358	    redaction_count: int = Field(ge=0)
   359	    manifest_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   360	
   361	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   362	    def validate_manifest_hash(self) -> "ContextManifest":
   363	        if len(self.entries) != len(self.compression_receipts):
   364	            raise ValueError("each manifest entry requires a compression receipt")
   365	        if len({entry.stable_id for entry in self.entries}) != len(self.entries):
   366	            raise ValueError("manifest entry stable_id values must be unique")
   367	        if tuple(entry.stable_id for entry in self.entries) != tuple(
   368	            receipt.stable_id for receipt in self.compression_receipts
   369	        ):
   370	            raise ValueError("manifest entries and compression receipts must align")
   371	        material = self.model_dump(mode="json", exclude={"manifest_hash"})
   372	        if self.manifest_hash != content_hash(material):
   373	            raise ValueError("manifest_hash mismatch")
   374	        try:
   375	            redacted_envelope = json.loads(self.redacted_envelope_json)
   376	        except json.JSONDecodeError as exc:
   377	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_json must be canonical JSON") from exc
   378	        if self.redacted_envelope_json != canonical_json(redacted_envelope):
   379	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_json must be canonical JSON")
   380	        if self.redacted_envelope_hash != content_hash(redacted_envelope):
   381	            raise ValueError("redacted_envelope_hash mismatch")
   382	        envelope = ContextEnvelope.model_validate(redacted_envelope)
   383	        if envelope.content_hash != redacted_envelope.get("content_hash"):
   384	            raise ValueError("redacted envelope content hash mismatch")
   385	        required_artifact_refs = {
   386	            section.source.artifact_ref
   387	            for section in envelope.sections
   388	            if section.source.fetchable and section.source.artifact_ref is not None
   389	        }
   390	        provided_artifact_refs = set(self.artifact_refs)
   391	        missing = required_artifact_refs - provided_artifact_refs
   392	        if missing:
   393	            raise ValueError(
   394	                "artifact_refs must include every fetchable source's "
   395	                f"artifact_ref; missing: {sorted(missing)}"
   396	            )
   397	        return self
   398	
   399	    def reconstruct_messages(self) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   400	        return [json.loads(entry.payload_json) for entry in self.entries if entry.surface == "message"]
   401	
   402	    def reconstruct_tool_schemas(self) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   403	        schemas = [json.loads(entry.payload_json) for entry in self.entries if entry.surface == "tool_schemas"]
   404	        return [schema for group in schemas for schema in group]
   405	
   406	    def reconstruct_redacted_envelope(self) -> ContextEnvelope:
   407	        return ContextEnvelope.model_validate_json(self.redacted_envelope_json)
    80	
    81	class LiveContextViolation(Exception):
    82	    """A live-context contract was violated — raised BEFORE any model call.
    83	
    84	    Deterministic: pure assembly with no infrastructure luck, so a retry would
    85	    fail identically. BaseRunner tags it as WorkerResult.error_kind =
    86	    "context_contract" (META-19 F6).
    87	    """
    88	
    89	
    90	class SectionDraft(FrozenModel):
    91	    """The caller-declared input to `assemble_live`: what one section IS.
    92	
    93	    Token counts and hashes are computed by the assembler, never declared. The
    94	    optional message-rendering hints (`role`, `tool_call_id`, `tool_calls`)
    95	    let assistant tool-call turns and tool observations round-trip losslessly
    96	    (F4) so round-N request bodies are exactly reconstructable.
    97	    """
    98	
    99	    section_type: ContextSectionType
   100	    source_kind: ContextSourceKind
   101	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   102	    trust: ContextTrust
   103	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   104	    content: str = ""
   105	    role: Optional[str] = None  # system/user/assistant/tool; None renders as user
   106	    tool_call_id: Optional[str] = None
   107	    tool_calls: Optional[list[dict[str, Any]]] = None
   108	
   109	
   110	class LiveAssembly(BaseModel):
   111	    """Every transport surface for one assembly, all redacted, plus provenance.
   112	
   113	    `_body()` / CLI argv MUST consume THESE surfaces, never the raw originals —
   114	    that is what makes redaction cover the bytes actually sent.
   115	    """
   116	
   117	    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid", frozen=True, arbitrary_types_allowed=True)
   118	    messages: list[dict[str, Any]]
   119	    tool_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]]
   120	    prompt: str
   121	    system_prompt: str
   122	    envelope: ContextEnvelope
   123	    manifest: ContextManifest
   124	
   125	
   126	def _mergeable(role: str, draft: SectionDraft) -> bool:
   127	    """system/user text drafts merge into one message; assistant/tool turns
   128	    (structured extras) each stay a discrete message."""
   129	    return role in ("system", "user") and not draft.tool_calls and not draft.tool_call_id
   130	
   131	
   132	def _group_messages(rendered: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
   133	    """Group rendered drafts into per-message groups, merging consecutive
   134	    same-role text turns. Each group renders to exactly one chat message."""
   135	    groups: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   136	    for item in rendered:
   137	        erole = item["role"] or "user"
   138	        if (groups and item["merge"] and groups[-1]["merge"]
   139	                and groups[-1]["erole"] == erole):
   140	            groups[-1]["items"].append(item)
   141	        else:
   142	            groups.append({"erole": erole, "merge": item["merge"], "items": [item]})
   143	    return groups
   144	
   145	
   146	def _render_group(group: dict[str, Any], key: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
   147	    """Render one message group to a chat message using content variant `key`
   148	    ('final' for the sent bytes, 'pre' for the pre-fit comparison)."""
   149	    message: dict[str, Any] = {
   150	        "role": group["erole"],
   151	        "content": "\n\n".join(item[key] for item in group["items"]),
   152	    }
   153	    first = group["items"][0]
   154	    if first["tool_calls"] is not None:  # only ever a single-item structured turn
   155	        message["tool_calls"] = first["tool_calls"]
   156	    if first["tool_call_id"] is not None:
   157	        message["tool_call_id"] = first["tool_call_id"]
   158	    return message
   159	
   160	
   161	def assemble_live(
   162	    drafts: list[SectionDraft],
   163	    *,
   164	    budget_tokens: int,
   165	    model_id: str,
   166	    harness_version: str,
   167	    tier: Tier,
   168	    redaction_values: Iterable[str] = (),
   169	    tool_schemas: Optional[list[dict[str, Any]]] = None,
   170	    policy_version: str = "context-live-v1",
   171	    memory_snapshot_version: Optional[str] = None,
   172	    evaluator_version: str = "not-bound:live",
   173	    weight_snapshot_version: Optional[str] = None,
   174	    evidence_snapshot_version: str = "not-bound:live",
   175	    candidate_version: str = "live-prompt",
   176	    parent_candidate_version: Optional[str] = None,
   177	    model_portfolio_version: str = "not-bound:live",
   178	    project_id: str = "meta-harness",
   179	) -> LiveAssembly:
   180	    """Assemble one live context, fail-closed. Raises `LiveContextViolation`
   181	    (pre model call) on any trust or budget contract breach.
   182	
   183	    F9 documented non-goal: never pass a '-breaking-' `harness_version` here —
   184	    `ContextVersionBindings` demands `evidence_snapshot_version=None` for a
   185	    breaking bump, but that field is non-nullable (models.py:103 vs :111). The
   186	    live path binds concrete snapshot versions, so a breaking bump would raise a
   187	    bare pydantic error; the frozen validator is intentionally left untouched.
   188	    """
   189	    # -- a. trust enforcement (fail closed) -----------------------------------
   190	    seen_ids: set[str] = set()
   191	    for draft in drafts:
   192	        if draft.stable_id in seen_ids:
   193	            raise LiveContextViolation(f"duplicate section stable_id {draft.stable_id!r}")
   194	        seen_ids.add(draft.stable_id)
   195	        if draft.section_type in _INSTRUCTION_SLOTS and draft.trust is not ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION:
   196	            raise LiveContextViolation(
   197	                f"instruction slot {draft.section_type.value!r} requires INSTRUCTION "
   198	                f"trust, got {draft.trust.value!r} (section {draft.stable_id!r})"
   199	            )
   200	        if (
   201	            draft.trust in (ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE, ContextTrust.GENERATED_SUMMARY)
   202	            and draft.section_type in _INSTRUCTION_SLOTS
   203	        ):
   204	            raise LiveContextViolation(
   205	                f"{draft.trust.value!r} content may never occupy instruction slot "
   206	                f"{draft.section_type.value!r} (section {draft.stable_id!r})"
   207	            )
   208	        if (
   209	            draft.source_kind is ContextSourceKind.EVALUATOR_RECEIPT
   210	            and draft.trust is ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION
   211	        ):
   212	            # ContextSourceRef enforces this too; surface it as the typed live
   213	            # violation rather than a bare pydantic error (spec 1a).
   214	            raise LiveContextViolation(
   215	                f"evaluator_receipt sources may never carry INSTRUCTION trust "
   216	                f"(section {draft.stable_id!r})"
   217	            )
   218	
   219	    redaction_tuple = tuple(sorted(
   220	        {value for value in redaction_values if value},
   221	        key=lambda value: (-len(value), value),
   222	    ))
   223	
   224	    # -- b. redaction on live content (before fitting) + c. per-section fit ----
   225	    section_budgets = allocate_section_budgets(
   226	        [draft.section_type for draft in drafts], budget_tokens, tier
   227	    )
   228	    sections: list[ContextSection] = []
   229	    rendered: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   230	    redaction_count = 0
   231	    for index, draft in enumerate(drafts):
   232	        redacted_content, ccount = _redact_string(draft.content, redaction_tuple)
   233	        redacted_tool_calls: Optional[list[dict[str, Any]]] = None
   234	        if draft.tool_calls is not None:
   235	            redacted_tool_calls, tcount = _redact(draft.tool_calls, redaction_tuple)
   236	            ccount += tcount
   237	        redaction_count += ccount
   238	
   239	        budget = section_budgets[index]
   240	        protected = draft.section_type in _PROTECTED_SECTIONS
   241	        redacted_tokens = estimate_tokens(redacted_content)
   242	        if redacted_tokens <= budget:
   243	            final_content, action = redacted_content, CompressionAction.NONE
   244	        elif budget <= 0 and not protected and redacted_content:
   245	            # non-protected zero-budget section: omit honestly (spec 1c)
   246	            final_content, action = "", CompressionAction.OMITTED
   247	        else:
   248	            # deterministic head/tail digest to the section's char budget; may
   249	            # GROW a tiny input near the floor (pruning marker) — recorded
   250	            # honestly as HEAD_TAIL only when the content actually changed.
   251	            candidate = digest_text(redacted_content, max(1, budget * 4))
   252	            if candidate == redacted_content:
   253	                final_content, action = redacted_content, CompressionAction.NONE
   254	            else:
   255	                final_content, action = candidate, CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL
   256	
   257	        # original >= selected so the models.py count invariant holds even when
   258	        # redaction's placeholder grows a tiny secret (selected = post-redaction).
   259	        original_tokens = max(estimate_tokens(draft.content), redacted_tokens)
   260	        selected_tokens = redacted_tokens
   261	        if action is CompressionAction.OMITTED:
   262	            compressed_tokens = 0
   263	            reason: Optional[str] = "zero token budget after tier allocation"
   264	        elif action is CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL:
   265	            compressed_tokens = estimate_tokens(final_content)
   266	            reason = "deterministic head/tail budget fitting"
   267	        else:
   268	            compressed_tokens = selected_tokens
   269	            reason = None
   270	
   271	        content_h = content_hash(final_content)
   272	        source = ContextSourceRef(
   273	            source_id=draft.stable_id,
   274	            kind=draft.source_kind,
   275	            scope=ContextScope(project_id=project_id),
   276	            trust=draft.trust,
   277	            content_hash=content_h,
   278	            selection_reason="live context assembly (META-19)",
   279	            sensitivity=draft.sensitivity,
   280	            fetchable=False,
   281	        )
   282	        sections.append(ContextSection(
   283	            section_type=draft.section_type,
   284	            stable_id=draft.stable_id,
   285	            source=source,
   286	            source_hash=content_h,
   287	            trust=draft.trust,
   288	            content=final_content,
   289	            original_tokens=original_tokens,
   290	            selected_tokens=selected_tokens,
   291	            compressed_tokens=compressed_tokens,
   292	            budget_tokens=budget,
   293	            ordering_priority=index,
   294	            sensitivity=draft.sensitivity,
   295	            redaction_markers=("[REDACTED]",) if ccount else (),
   296	            compression_action=action,
   297	            omission_reason=reason,
   298	        ))
   299	        role = draft.role or "user"
   300	        rendered.append({
   301	            "draft": draft,
   302	            "role": draft.role,
   303	            "merge": _mergeable(role, draft),
   304	            "pre": redacted_content,
   305	            "final": final_content,
   306	            "source_content": draft.content,
   307	            "tool_calls": redacted_tool_calls,
   308	            "tool_call_id": draft.tool_call_id,
   309	            "redacted": ccount > 0,
   310	        })
   311	
   312	    # -- d. envelope ----------------------------------------------------------
   313	    versions = ContextVersionBindings(
   314	        model_portfolio_version=model_portfolio_version,
   315	        harness_version=harness_version,
   316	        evaluator_version=evaluator_version,
   317	        weight_snapshot_version=weight_snapshot_version,
   318	        memory_snapshot_version=memory_snapshot_version,
   319	        evidence_snapshot_version=evidence_snapshot_version,
   320	        candidate_version=candidate_version,
   321	        parent_candidate_version=parent_candidate_version,
   322	    )
   323	    envelope = _make_envelope(
   324	        sections, policy_version=policy_version, model_id=model_id, versions=versions,
   325	    )
   326	
   327	    # -- transport surfaces (all redacted) ------------------------------------
   328	    groups = _group_messages(rendered)
   329	    messages = [_render_group(group, "final") for group in groups]
   330	    messages_pre = [_render_group(group, "pre") for group in groups]
   331	    non_system = [item for item in rendered if (item["role"] or "user") != "system"]
   332	    system_items = [item for item in rendered if item["role"] == "system"]
   333	    prompt = "\n\n".join(item["final"] for item in non_system)
   334	    prompt_pre = "\n\n".join(item["pre"] for item in non_system)
   335	    system_prompt = "\n\n".join(item["final"] for item in system_items)
   336	    system_prompt_pre = "\n\n".join(item["pre"] for item in system_items)
   337	
   338	    redacted_schemas: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
   339	    tool_schema_tokens = 0
   340	    if tool_schemas:
   341	        schema_payload = [dict(schema) for schema in tool_schemas]
   342	        redacted_schemas, scount = _redact(schema_payload, redaction_tuple)
   343	        redaction_count += scount
   344	        tool_schema_tokens = estimate_tokens(canonical_json(redacted_schemas))
   345	
   346	    # -- e. hard budget postcondition (F7) ------------------------------------
   347	    messages_total = messages_tokens(messages) + tool_schema_tokens
   348	    cli_total = estimate_tokens(prompt) + estimate_tokens(system_prompt)
   349	    if max(messages_total, cli_total) > budget_tokens:
   350	        raise LiveContextViolation(
   351	            f"assembled context exceeds hard budget: max surface "
   352	            f"{max(messages_total, cli_total)} > {budget_tokens} tokens "
   353	            "(protected sections cannot be omitted to fit)"
   354	        )
   355	
   356	    # -- manifest entries + 1:1 compression receipts --------------------------
   357	    entries: list[ContextManifestEntry] = []
   358	    receipts: list[CompressionReceipt] = []
   359	    # message surfaces: one entry per rendered message. A merged message spans
   360	    # drafts of possibly differing trust — report the weakest (untrusted wins).
   361	    for group, message, message_pre in zip(groups, messages, messages_pre, strict=True):
   362	        members: list[dict[str, Any]] = group["items"]
   363	        weakest = min(members, key=lambda item: _TRUST_WEAKNESS[item["draft"].trust])
   364	        sensitivity = max(
   365	            (item["draft"].sensitivity for item in members),
   366	            key=lambda value: _SENSITIVITY_RANK[value],
   367	        )
   368	        stable_id = f"message-{len(entries):04d}-{message['role']}"
   369	        payload = {key: value for key, value in message.items()}
   370	        payload_pre = {key: value for key, value in message_pre.items()}
   371	        before_hash = content_hash(payload_pre)
   372	        after_hash = content_hash(payload)
   373	        action = CompressionAction.NONE if before_hash == after_hash else CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL
   374	        source_hash = content_hash("".join(item["source_content"] for item in members))
   375	        entries.append(ContextManifestEntry(
   376	            stable_id=stable_id,
   377	            surface="message",
   378	            payload_json=canonical_json(payload),
   379	            source_kind=weakest["draft"].source_kind,
   380	            trust=weakest["draft"].trust,
   381	            sensitivity=sensitivity,
   382	            source_hash=source_hash,
   383	            selected_hash=content_hash(payload),
   384	            redacted=any(item["redacted"] for item in members),
   385	        ))
   386	        receipts.append(CompressionReceipt(
   387	            stable_id=stable_id,
   388	            action=action,
   389	            before_hash=before_hash,
   390	            after_hash=after_hash,
   391	            original_tokens=estimate_tokens(str(message_pre.get("content") or "")),
   392	            final_tokens=estimate_tokens(str(message.get("content") or "")),
   393	            reason="within allocated budget" if action is CompressionAction.NONE
   394	            else "deterministic head/tail budget fitting",
   395	        ))
   396	
   397	    def _string_surface_entry(surface: str, stable_id: str, pre: str, final: str,
   398	                              members: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> None:
   399	        before_hash, after_hash = content_hash(pre), content_hash(final)
   400	        action = (CompressionAction.NONE if before_hash == after_hash
   401	                  else CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL)
   402	        weakest = min(members, key=lambda item: _TRUST_WEAKNESS[item["draft"].trust])
   403	        sensitivity = max(
   404	            (item["draft"].sensitivity for item in members),
   405	            key=lambda value: _SENSITIVITY_RANK[value],
   406	        )
   407	        entries.append(ContextManifestEntry(
   408	            stable_id=stable_id,
   409	            surface=surface,  # type: ignore[arg-type]
   410	            payload_json=canonical_json(final),
   411	            source_kind=weakest["draft"].source_kind,
   412	            trust=weakest["draft"].trust,
   413	            sensitivity=sensitivity,
   414	            source_hash=content_hash("".join(item["source_content"] for item in members)),
   415	            selected_hash=content_hash(final),
   416	            redacted=any(item["redacted"] for item in members),
   417	        ))
   418	        receipts.append(CompressionReceipt(
   419	            stable_id=stable_id,
   420	            action=action,
   421	            before_hash=before_hash,
   422	            after_hash=after_hash,
   423	            original_tokens=estimate_tokens(pre),
   424	            final_tokens=estimate_tokens(final),
   425	            reason="within allocated budget" if action is CompressionAction.NONE
   426	            else "deterministic head/tail budget fitting",
   427	        ))
   428	
   429	    if tool_schemas:
   430	        schema_json = canonical_json(redacted_schemas)
   431	        before = content_hash([dict(schema) for schema in tool_schemas])
   432	        after = content_hash(redacted_schemas)
   433	        action = CompressionAction.NONE if before == after else CompressionAction.HEAD_TAIL
   434	        # tool schemas are transported verbatim (never fitted); redaction may
   435	        # differ them but that is not compression — record NONE with equal
   436	        # hashes on the redacted payload to keep the receipt honest.
   437	        entries.append(ContextManifestEntry(
   438	            stable_id="tool-schemas",
   439	            surface="tool_schemas",
   440	            payload_json=schema_json,
   441	            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.TOOL_POLICY_SCHEMA,
   442	            trust=ContextTrust.INSTRUCTION,
   443	            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
   444	            source_hash=after,
   445	            selected_hash=content_hash(redacted_schemas),
   446	            redacted=before != after,
   447	        ))
   448	        receipts.append(CompressionReceipt(
   449	            stable_id="tool-schemas",
   450	            action=CompressionAction.NONE,
   451	            before_hash=after,
   452	            after_hash=after,
   453	            original_tokens=tool_schema_tokens,
   454	            final_tokens=tool_schema_tokens,
   455	            reason="tool schemas transported within allocated budget",
   456	        ))
   457	
   458	    # flat prompt is always a derivable CLI surface; system prompt only when at
   459	    # least one system-role draft was declared (else claiming it would be false).
   460	    _string_surface_entry("flat_prompt", "flat-prompt", prompt_pre, prompt,
   461	                          non_system or rendered)
   462	    if system_items:
   463	        _string_surface_entry("system_prompt", "system-prompt", system_prompt_pre,
   464	                              system_prompt, system_items)
   465	
   466	    # -- manifest -------------------------------------------------------------
   467	    # sections are already redacted, so the envelope IS the redacted envelope.
   468	    redacted_envelope = envelope.model_dump(mode="json")
   469	    redacted_envelope_json = canonical_json(redacted_envelope)
   470	    manifest_values = {
   471	        "schema_version": 1,
   472	        "policy_version": policy_version,
   473	        "model_id": model_id,
   474	        "versions": versions,
   475	        "envelope_hash": envelope.content_hash,
   476	        "redacted_envelope_hash": content_hash(redacted_envelope),
   477	        "redacted_envelope_json": redacted_envelope_json,
   478	        "entries": tuple(entries),
   479	        "compression_receipts": tuple(receipts),
   480	        "source_candidates_considered": tuple(entry.stable_id for entry in entries),
   481	        "visibility_decisions": tuple(f"{entry.stable_id}:included" for entry in entries),
   482	        "deliberate_omissions": tuple(
   483	            section.stable_id for section in sections
   484	            if section.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED
   485	        ),
   486	        "artifact_refs": (),
   487	        "budget_used_tokens": messages_total,
   488	        "budget_limit_tokens": budget_tokens,
   489	        "redaction_count": redaction_count,
   490	    }
   491	    serializable = {
   492	        **manifest_values,
   493	        "versions": versions.model_dump(mode="json"),
   494	        "entries": [entry.model_dump(mode="json") for entry in entries],
   495	        "compression_receipts": [receipt.model_dump(mode="json") for receipt in receipts],
   496	    }
   497	    manifest = ContextManifest(**manifest_values, manifest_hash=content_hash(serializable))
   498	
   499	    return LiveAssembly(
   500	        messages=messages,
   501	        tool_schemas=redacted_schemas,
   502	        prompt=prompt,
   503	        system_prompt=system_prompt,
   504	        envelope=envelope,
   505	        manifest=manifest,
   506	    )
