src/metaharness/core/types.py:159:    # detached signature over `result_signing_bytes(...)`, made with the worker's
     1	"""The uniform Runner interface every worker harness sits behind.
     2	
     3	The orchestrator never talks to a model directly — it talks to a Runner: a Task
     4	goes in, a WorkerResult comes out. Real LLM-backed harnesses, scripted mocks, and
     5	enrichment wrappers all present this same face, so the router and orchestrator can
     6	compose them freely.
     7	
     8	`BaseRunner.run` owns the cross-cutting concerns (OTel span, timing, error
     9	capture, result signing); concrete runners implement `_execute` only.
    10	"""
    11	from __future__ import annotations
    12	
    13	import time
    14	from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
    15	from typing import Optional
    16	
    17	from metaharness.core.types import Task, Tier, WorkerResult
    18	from metaharness.identity.canonical import canonical_bytes
    19	from metaharness.identity.keys import KeyPair
    20	from metaharness.identity.registry import WorkerRegistry
    21	from metaharness.observability.tracing import tracer
    22	
    23	
    24	class WorkerTimeout(RuntimeError):
    25	    """A worker's `_execute` ran out of its allotted wall-clock time. Carries
    26	    the timeout actually applied (post task-type scaling / config override,
    27	    issue #2) so callers can report it without re-deriving it."""
    28	
    29	    def __init__(self, msg: str, timeout_s: float) -> None:
    30	        super().__init__(msg)
    31	        self.timeout_s = timeout_s
    32	
    33	
    34	CURRENT_RESULT_SIGNATURE_VERSION = 2
    35	
    36	
    37	def result_signing_bytes(result: WorkerResult, *, version: Optional[int] = None) -> bytes:
    38	    """The exact bytes a worker signs to vouch for a result.
    39	
    40	    Version 1 is the historical payload and remains readable so old journals do
    41	    not become unverifiable. Version 2 additionally attests ``workspace_root``
    42	    and ``timed_out``: both now affect control flow (automatic test execution and
    43	    timeout classification), so treating them as mutable bookkeeping would let a
    44	    valid signature bless attacker-selected behavior.
    45	    """
    46	    version = result.signature_version if version is None else version
    47	    payload = {
    48	        "kind": "worker_result",
    49	        "task_id": result.task_id,
    50	        "worker_id": result.worker_id,
    51	        "model": result.model,
    52	        "output": result.output,
    53	        "raw_text": result.raw_text,
    54	        "error": result.error,
    55	    }
    56	    if version == 2:
    57	        payload.update({
    58	            "signature_version": 2,
    59	            "timed_out": result.timed_out,
    60	            "workspace_root": result.workspace_root,
    61	        })
    62	    elif version != 1:
    63	        raise ValueError(f"unsupported worker-result signature version {version}")
    64	    return canonical_bytes(payload)
    65	
    66	
    67	def sign_result(result: WorkerResult, keypair: KeyPair) -> WorkerResult:
    68	    """(Re)sign a result in place. Enrichment wrappers that legitimately rewrite
    69	    a worker's output inside the same harness boundary re-sign with the worker's
    70	    own key so the signature keeps matching what is actually returned."""
    71	    result.signature_version = CURRENT_RESULT_SIGNATURE_VERSION
    72	    result.signature_b64 = keypair.sign(result_signing_bytes(result))
    73	    return result
    74	
    75	
    76	def verify_result(result: WorkerResult, registry: WorkerRegistry) -> bool:
    77	    """True iff the result carries a signature that verifies under the key
    78	    registered for its worker_id."""
    79	    if not result.signature_b64:
    80	        return False
    81	    try:
    82	        payload = result_signing_bytes(result)
    83	    except ValueError:
    84	        return False
    85	    return registry.verify_message(result.worker_id, payload, result.signature_b64)
    86	
    87	
    88	class Runner(ABC):
    89	    """Anything that can execute a Task. Wrappers wrap Runners and are Runners."""
    90	
    91	    worker_id: str
    92	    tier: Tier
    93	    model: str
    94	
    95	    @abstractmethod
    96	    async def run(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult: ...
    97	
    98	
    99	class BaseRunner(Runner):
   100	    """Span + timing + signing wrapper around a concrete `_execute`."""
   101	
   102	    def __init__(
   103	        self,
   104	        worker_id: str,
   105	        tier: Tier,
   106	        model: str,
   107	        keypair: Optional[KeyPair] = None,
   108	    ) -> None:
   109	        self.worker_id = worker_id
   110	        self.tier = tier
   111	        self.model = model
   112	        self.keypair = keypair
   113	
   114	    async def run(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   115	        with tracer().start_as_current_span("worker.run") as span:
   116	            span.set_attribute("worker.id", self.worker_id)
   117	            span.set_attribute("worker.tier", self.tier.value)
   118	            span.set_attribute("worker.model", self.model)
   119	            span.set_attribute("task.id", task.id)
   120	            span.set_attribute("task.type", task.task_type.value)
   121	            started = time.monotonic()
   122	            try:
   123	                result = await self._execute(task)
   124	            except Exception as exc:  # a failed attempt is data, not a crash
   125	                # META-19 (F6): a live-context contract violation is deterministic
   126	                # (pure assembly, no infrastructure luck) — tag it so the executor
   127	                # aborts retries and excludes it from capability evidence. Imported
   128	                # lazily to avoid a harness->context import cycle at module load.
   129	                from metaharness.context.live import LiveContextViolation
   130	
   131	                error_kind = "context_contract" if isinstance(exc, LiveContextViolation) else None
   132	                result = WorkerResult(
   133	                    task_id=task.id,
   134	                    worker_id=self.worker_id,
   135	                    tier=self.tier,
   136	                    model=self.model,
   137	                    error=f"{type(exc).__name__}: {exc}",
   138	                    error_kind=error_kind,
   139	                    timed_out=isinstance(exc, WorkerTimeout),  # issue #2
   140	                )
   141	            result.latency_s = time.monotonic() - started
   142	            if self.keypair is not None:
   143	                sign_result(result, self.keypair)
   144	            span.set_attribute("worker.tokens_in", result.tokens_in)
   145	            span.set_attribute("worker.tokens_out", result.tokens_out)
   146	            span.set_attribute("worker.cost_usd", result.cost_usd)
   147	            if result.error:
   148	                span.set_attribute("worker.error", result.error)
   149	            return result
   150

 succeeded in 0ms:
     1	"""Worker registry: which workers the orchestrator knows, and which key vouches
     2	for each one.
     3	
     4	Registration is a challenge-response ceremony, the same shape as proving you own
     5	an SSH key: the registry hands out a one-time nonce, the worker signs
     6	{worker_id, public_key, nonce} with its private key, and the registry admits the
     7	worker only if that signature verifies under the presented public key. From then
     8	on, any message claiming to come from that worker can be checked against the
     9	registered key — authenticity, exactly like a verified commit.
    10	"""
    11	from __future__ import annotations
    12	
    13	import secrets
    14	import time
    15	from typing import Any, Optional
    16	
    17	from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
    18	
    19	from metaharness.identity.canonical import canonical_bytes
    20	from metaharness.identity.keys import verify
    21	
    22	
    23	class WorkerRecord(BaseModel):
    24	    """One admitted worker. `public_key_b64` is the identity anchor."""
    25	
    26	    worker_id: str
    27	    display_name: str = ""
    28	    public_key_b64: str
    29	    tiers: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    30	    task_types: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    31	    roles: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    32	    capabilities: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    33	    host: str = ""
    34	    active: bool = True
    35	    registered_at: float = 0.0
    36	    key_rotations: int = 0
    37	    metadata: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)
    38	
    39	
    40	class RegistrationChallenge(BaseModel):
    41	    worker_id: str
    42	    nonce: str
    43	    issued_at: float
    44	
    45	
    46	def registration_payload(worker_id: str, public_key_b64: str, nonce: str) -> bytes:
    47	    """The exact bytes a worker signs to complete registration."""
    48	    return canonical_bytes(
    49	        {"kind": "registration", "worker_id": worker_id, "public_key": public_key_b64, "nonce": nonce}
    50	    )
    51	
    52	
    53	def rotation_payload(worker_id: str, new_public_key_b64: str) -> bytes:
    54	    """The exact bytes a worker signs (with its *current* key) to rotate to a new key."""
    55	    return canonical_bytes(
    56	        {"kind": "key_rotation", "worker_id": worker_id, "new_public_key": new_public_key_b64}
    57	    )
    58	
    59	
    60	class RegistryError(Exception):
    61	    """Registration or lookup failed for a stated reason."""
    62	
    63	
    64	class WorkerRegistry:
    65	    """In-memory registry of admitted workers.
    66	
    67	    Flow: `begin_registration` → worker signs `registration_payload` →
    68	    `complete_registration`. Nonces are single-use and expire, so a captured
    69	    registration message can't be replayed later.
    70	    """
    71	
    72	    def __init__(self, challenge_ttl_s: float = 300.0) -> None:
    73	        self._workers: dict[str, WorkerRecord] = {}
    74	        self._challenges: dict[str, RegistrationChallenge] = {}
    75	        self._challenge_ttl_s = challenge_ttl_s
    76	
    77	    # -- registration ceremony -------------------------------------------------
    78	
    79	    def begin_registration(self, worker_id: str) -> RegistrationChallenge:
    80	        existing = self._workers.get(worker_id)
    81	        if existing is not None and existing.active:
    82	            raise RegistryError(f"worker {worker_id!r} is already registered")
    83	        # a retired (deactivated) id may be re-admitted with a fresh key: the
    84	        # ceremony runs again in full, and the old record's rotation count
    85	        # carries over so re-admission stays visible in the audit trail
    86	        challenge = RegistrationChallenge(
    87	            worker_id=worker_id, nonce=secrets.token_hex(16), issued_at=time.time()
    88	        )
    89	        self._challenges[worker_id] = challenge
    90	        return challenge
    91	
    92	    def complete_registration(
    93	        self,
    94	        worker_id: str,
    95	        public_key_b64: str,
    96	        signature_b64: str,
    97	        *,
    98	        display_name: str = "",
    99	        tiers: Optional[list[str]] = None,
   100	        task_types: Optional[list[str]] = None,
   101	        roles: Optional[list[str]] = None,
   102	        capabilities: Optional[list[str]] = None,
   103	        host: str = "",
   104	        metadata: Optional[dict[str, Any]] = None,
   105	        now: Optional[float] = None,
   106	    ) -> WorkerRecord:
   107	        at = now if now is not None else time.time()
   108	        challenge = self._challenges.get(worker_id)
   109	        if challenge is None:
   110	            raise RegistryError(f"no pending challenge for worker {worker_id!r}")
   111	        if at - challenge.issued_at > self._challenge_ttl_s:
   112	            del self._challenges[worker_id]
   113	            raise RegistryError(f"challenge for {worker_id!r} expired")
   114	        payload = registration_payload(worker_id, public_key_b64, challenge.nonce)
   115	        if not verify(public_key_b64, payload, signature_b64):
   116	            raise RegistryError(
   117	                f"registration signature for {worker_id!r} does not verify under the presented key"
   118	            )
   119	        del self._challenges[worker_id]  # single-use
   120	        previous = self._workers.get(worker_id)
   121	        record = WorkerRecord(
   122	            worker_id=worker_id,
   123	            display_name=display_name or worker_id,
   124	            public_key_b64=public_key_b64,
   125	            tiers=tiers or [],
   126	            task_types=task_types or [],
   127	            roles=roles or [],
   128	            capabilities=capabilities or [],
   129	            host=host,
   130	            registered_at=at,
   131	            key_rotations=(previous.key_rotations + 1) if previous else 0,
   132	            metadata=metadata or {},
   133	        )
   134	        self._workers[worker_id] = record
   135	        return record
   136	
   137	    # -- lookups ---------------------------------------------------------------
   138	
   139	    def get(self, worker_id: str) -> Optional[WorkerRecord]:
   140	        return self._workers.get(worker_id)
   141	
   142	    def all(self) -> list[WorkerRecord]:
   143	        return list(self._workers.values())
   144	
   145	    def is_active(self, worker_id: str) -> bool:
   146	        record = self._workers.get(worker_id)
   147	        return bool(record and record.active)
   148	
   149	    # -- ongoing authenticity checks --------------------------------------------
   150	
   151	    def verify_message(self, worker_id: str, message: bytes, signature_b64: str) -> bool:
   152	        """True iff `message` was signed by the key registered for `worker_id`
   153	        and the worker is currently active."""
   154	        record = self._workers.get(worker_id)
   155	        if record is None or not record.active:
   156	            return False
   157	        return verify(record.public_key_b64, message, signature_b64)
   158	
   159	    def rotate_key(self, worker_id: str, new_public_key_b64: str, signature_b64: str) -> WorkerRecord:
   160	        """Swap a worker's key. The rotation request must be signed by the
   161	        *current* registered key — continuity of identity, like signing a new
   162	        GPG key with the old one."""
   163	        record = self._workers.get(worker_id)
   164	        if record is None:
   165	            raise RegistryError(f"worker {worker_id!r} is not registered")
   166	        payload = rotation_payload(worker_id, new_public_key_b64)
   167	        if not verify(record.public_key_b64, payload, signature_b64):
   168	            raise RegistryError(f"key rotation for {worker_id!r} not signed by current key")
   169	        record.public_key_b64 = new_public_key_b64
   170	        record.key_rotations += 1
   171	        return record
   172	
   173	    def deactivate(self, worker_id: str) -> None:
   174	        record = self._workers.get(worker_id)
   175	        if record is None:
   176	            raise RegistryError(f"worker {worker_id!r} is not registered")
   177	        record.active = False
   178	
   179	    def reactivate(self, worker_id: str) -> None:
   180	        record = self._workers.get(worker_id)

   246	async def test_context_contract_violation_aborts_retries_and_is_no_capability_evidence():
   247	    """META-19 (F6): a deterministic LiveContextViolation surfaces as
   248	    error_kind="context_contract". Retries are pure waste (same inputs would
   249	    reproduce it), so the task aborts after one attempt, and the failure never
   250	    banks capability/routing evidence (it is not a model-skill signal)."""

   252	    from metaharness.harness.runner import BaseRunner

   255	        def __init__(self):
   256	            super().__init__(worker_id="w", tier=Tier.SMALL, model="model-a")
   257	            self.calls = 0
   258	
   259	        async def _execute(self, task: Task) -> WorkerResult:
   260	            self.calls += 1
   261	            raise LiveContextViolation("untrusted content in instruction slot")
   262	
   263	    matrix = CapabilityMatrix()
   264	    worker = ViolatingWorker()

   266	    outcome = await executor.execute(classify_task(max_attempts=3))
   267

   272	    assert matrix.samples("model-a", TaskType.CLASSIFY) == 0  # excluded from evidence

   170	    Evidence (arXiv 2512.24103): intrinsic self-critique lifts planning-shaped
   171	    work when it is *iterative* — draft → critique → revise — not "think again".
   172	    And per arXiv 2606.05976, the draft is presented to the critic and the
   173	    reviser as an external artifact ("a worker produced this"), which is the
   174	    framing models actually correct against.
   175	
   176	    Only fires where the verifier would return UNVERIFIED (no success_check, no
   177	    schema) and the task type is open-ended; checkable tasks keep their cheaper

   165	class PromptDirectives(_Wrapper):
   166	    """Additive prompt-space search: append candidate directives to the task's
   167	    boundaries (the delegation contract) without touching anything else."""
   168	
   169	    def __init__(self, inner: Runner, directives: list[str]) -> None:
   170	        super().__init__(inner)
   171	        self.directives = list(directives)
   172	
   173	    async def run(self, task):
   174	        amended = task.model_copy(deep=True)
   175	        amended.boundaries = list(task.boundaries) + self.directives
   176	        result = await self.inner.run(amended)
   177	        result.task_id = task.id
   178	        return result

   181	# Knob documentation handed to the LLM proposer — kept next to the fields so a
   182	# new knob can't ship without the proposer learning it exists.
   183	KNOB_DOCS = """\
   184	Tunable knobs (the delta may set any subset):
   185	- tool_offload (bool): PAL — arithmetic tasks emit a program that is evaluated
   186	  exactly instead of computed by the model. Helps when arithmetic answers are wrong.
   187	- self_consistency_k (int, 1..7): sample k answers, majority-vote. Helps when wrong
   188	  answers scatter across attempts. Multiplies token cost by ~k.
   189	- schema_guard_retries (int, 0..3): re-ask naming schema violations. Helps when
   190	  failures are schema-shaped (missing keys, wrong types).
   191	- self_critique_rounds (int, 0..2): draft->critique->revise for tasks with NO
   192	  checkable signal. Useless on deterministic eval suites; costs tokens.
   193	- prompt_directives (list of <=4 strings, <=300 chars each): ADDITIVE instructions
   194	  appended to every task's boundaries. Never rewrites existing prompts."""
    50	    max_attempts: int = 3
    51	    depends_on: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)
    52	    hitl: bool = False    # require human approval at hitl_timing
    53	    hitl_timing: Literal["before", "after"] = "before"
    54	    tools: list[str] = Field(default_factory=list)  # tool subset for this step
    55	    requires_execution_evidence: bool = False
    56	    # conditional execution: {"step": "<id>", "equals"|"contains"|"one_of": value,
    57	    # "negate": bool} — evaluated deterministically against the referenced step's
    58	    # output at advance-time; unmet -> this step is journaled as skipped

    61	    @model_validator(mode="after")
    62	    def _assignment_is_unambiguous(self) -> "StepSpec":
    63	        self.role = (self.role.strip() or None) if self.role else None
    64	        self.worker_id = (self.worker_id.strip() or None) if self.worker_id else None
    65	        self.required_capabilities = list(dict.fromkeys(
    66	            value.strip() for value in self.required_capabilities if value.strip()
    67	        ))
    68	        if self.worker_id and self.tier_hint is not None:
    69	            raise ValueError("worker_id and tier_hint cannot be combined")
    70	        return self
    71	
    72	    def to_task(
    73	        self,
    74	        resolved_inputs: dict[str, Any],
    75	        *,
    76	        objective: str | None = None,
    77	        boundaries: list[str] | None = None,
    78	    ) -> Task:
    79	        boundaries = list(self.boundaries if boundaries is None else boundaries)
    80	        # a one_of check is a format contract the worker deserves to see spelled
    81	        # out — exact-match verification punishes prose around a right answer
    82	        if self.success_check and "one_of" in self.success_check:
    83	            allowed = ", ".join(repr(v) for v in self.success_check["one_of"])
    84	            boundaries.append(
    85	                f"Respond with exactly one of the following values and nothing else: {allowed}."
    86	            )
    87	        return Task(
    88	            task_type=self.task_type,
    89	            objective=self.objective if objective is None else objective,
    90	            inputs=resolved_inputs,
    91	            output_schema=self.output_schema,
    92	            boundaries=boundaries,
    93	            success_check=self.success_check,
    94	            tier_hint=self.tier_hint,
    95	            role=self.role,
    96	            required_capabilities=list(self.required_capabilities),
    97	            worker_id=self.worker_id,
    98	            max_attempts=self.max_attempts,
    99	            tools=list(self.tools),
   100	            requires_execution_evidence=self.requires_execution_evidence,
   101	        )

   165	def load_workflow(source: str | Path) -> WorkflowSpec:
   166	    """Load a WorkflowSpec from a YAML file path or a YAML string."""
   167	    text = source
   168	    if isinstance(source, Path) or (isinstance(source, str) and "\n" not in source and source.endswith((".yml", ".yaml"))):
   169	        text = Path(source).read_text(encoding="utf-8")
   170	    data = yaml.safe_load(text)
   171	    return WorkflowSpec.model_validate(data)
   172	
   173	
   174	def resolve_reference(value: Any, context: dict[str, Any], outputs: dict[str, Any]) -> Any:
   175	    """Resolve `$context.key` / `$steps.id.output[.subkey...]` references in step
   176	    inputs. Non-string values and non-reference strings pass through untouched."""
   177	    if isinstance(value, dict):
   178	        return {k: resolve_reference(v, context, outputs) for k, v in value.items()}
   179	    if isinstance(value, list):
   180	        return [resolve_reference(v, context, outputs) for v in value]
   181	    if not isinstance(value, str) or not value.startswith("$"):
   182	        return value
   183	    parts = value[1:].split(".")
   184	    if parts[0] == "context":
   185	        node: Any = context
   186	        path = parts[1:]
   187	    elif parts[0] == "steps":
   188	        if len(parts) < 3 or parts[2] != "output":
   189	            raise ValueError(f"bad step reference {value!r}; use $steps.<id>.output[...]")
   190	        if parts[1] not in outputs:
   191	            raise ValueError(f"step reference {value!r} points to a step with no recorded output")
   192	        node = outputs[parts[1]]
   193	        path = parts[3:]
   194	    else:
   195	        raise ValueError(f"unknown reference root {value!r}")
   196	    for key in path:
   197	        if isinstance(node, dict) and key in node:
   198	            node = node[key]
   199	        else:
   200	            raise ValueError(f"reference {value!r}: {key!r} not found")
   201	    return node
   202	
   203	
   204	_INLINE_REF_RE = re.compile(r"\$(context(?:\.[A-Za-z0-9_-]+)+|steps\.[A-Za-z0-9_-]+\.output(?:\.[A-Za-z0-9_-]+)*)")
   205	
   206	
   207	def resolve_text_references(text: str, context: dict[str, Any], outputs: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
   208	    """Render references embedded in human-facing delegation text.
   209	
   210	    Step inputs keep exact-reference semantics so structured values stay
   211	    structured. Objectives and boundaries are prompt text, so embedded values
   212	    are stringified loudly before the task reaches a worker.
   213	    """
   214	    def substitute(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
   215	        return str(resolve_reference("$" + match.group(1), context, outputs))
   216	
   217	    return _INLINE_REF_RE.sub(substitute, text)
   218	
   219	
   220	def when_satisfied(when: dict[str, Any], outputs: dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
   221	    """Deterministic branch predicate: does the referenced step's output meet
   222	    the condition? A missing/skipped source counts as NOT satisfied."""
   223	    ref = when["step"]
   224	    if ref not in outputs:
   225	        return False

   180	class ContextSection(FrozenModel):
   181	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   182	    section_type: ContextSectionType
   183	    stable_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   184	    source: ContextSourceRef
   185	    source_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   186	    trust: ContextTrust
   187	    content: str
   188	    original_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   189	    selected_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   190	    compressed_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   191	    budget_tokens: int = Field(ge=0)
   192	    ordering_priority: int = Field(ge=0)
   193	    sensitivity: Sensitivity
   194	    redaction_markers: tuple[str, ...] = ()
   195	    compression_action: CompressionAction = CompressionAction.NONE
   196	    omission_reason: str | None = Field(default=None, min_length=1)
   197	    retrieval_score: float | None = None
   198	
   199	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   200	    def validate_provenance_and_counts(self) -> "ContextSection":
   201	        if self.source.content_hash is not None and self.source_hash != self.source.content_hash:
   202	            raise ValueError("source_hash must match source.content_hash")
   203	        if self.trust != self.source.trust:
   204	            raise ValueError("section trust must match source trust")
   205	        if self.sensitivity != self.source.sensitivity:
   206	            raise ValueError("section sensitivity must match source sensitivity")
   207	        if self.selected_tokens > self.original_tokens:
   208	            raise ValueError("selected token count cannot exceed original")
   209	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.NONE:
   210	            if self.omission_reason is not None:
   211	                raise ValueError("uncompressed sections cannot have an omission reason")
   212	            if self.compressed_tokens != self.selected_tokens:
   213	                raise ValueError("uncompressed token counts must match")
   214	        elif self.omission_reason is None:
   215	            raise ValueError("compression or omission requires a reason")
   216	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED and self.content:
   217	            raise ValueError("omitted sections cannot retain content")
   218	        if self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED and self.compressed_tokens != 0:
   219	            raise ValueError("omitted sections must have zero rendered tokens")
   220	        if self.section_type in {
   221	            ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
   222	            ContextSectionType.RESPONSE_CONTRACT,
   223	        } and self.compression_action is CompressionAction.OMITTED:
   224	            raise ValueError("protected edge sections cannot be omitted")
   225	        return self

   227	
   228	class ContextEnvelope(FrozenModel):
   229	    schema_version: Literal[1] = 1
   230	    policy_version: str = Field(min_length=1)
   231	    model_id: str = Field(min_length=1)
   232	    versions: ContextVersionBindings
   233	    sections: tuple[ContextSection, ...]
   234	    content_hash: str = Field(pattern=SHA256_PATTERN)
   235	
   236	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   237	    def validate_hash_and_order(self) -> "ContextEnvelope":
   238	        if len({section.stable_id for section in self.sections}) != len(self.sections):
   239	            raise ValueError("section stable_id values must be unique")
   240	        priorities = [section.ordering_priority for section in self.sections]
   241	        if priorities != list(range(len(self.sections))):
   242	            raise ValueError("sections must have unique contiguous priorities")
   243	        project_ids = {section.source.scope.project_id for section in self.sections}
   244	        if len(project_ids) > 1:
   245	            raise ValueError(
   246	                "envelope sections must share a single source scope "
   247	                "project_id (no cross-project scope bleed); got "
   248	                f"{sorted(project_ids)}"
   249	            )
   250	        identity_by_source_id: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
   251	        for section in self.sections:
   252	            mode = "pinned" if section.source.content_hash is not None else "live"
   253	            identity_by_source_id.setdefault(section.source.source_id, set()).add(mode)
   254	        for source_id, modes in identity_by_source_id.items():
   255	            if len(modes) > 1:
   256	                raise ValueError(
   257	                    f"envelope sections sharing source_id={source_id!r} mix "
   258	                    "pinned (content_hash) and live (high_water_mark) identity "
   259	                    "without an explicit reconciliation marker (future "
   260	                    "marker: not yet supported)"
   261	                )
   262	        material = self.model_dump(mode="json", exclude={"content_hash"})
   263	        if self.content_hash != content_hash(material):
   264	            raise ValueError("envelope content_hash mismatch")
   265	        return self

+async def test_local_trust_violation_makes_no_model_call(monkeypatch):
+    """META-19 (test 1): a trust violation on the worker path raises before the
+    endpoint is ever hit; the runner tags error_kind='context_contract'."""
+    from metaharness.harness import local as local_mod
+
+    calls = {"n": 0}
+
+    def handler(request: httpx.Request) -> httpx.Response:
+        calls["n"] += 1
+        return httpx.Response(200, json={"choices": [{"message": {"content": "x"}}]})
+
+    def bad_drafts(task, system_prompt=""):
+        return [SectionDraft(
+            section_type=ContextSectionType.SYSTEM_INSTRUCTIONS,
+            source_kind=ContextSourceKind.LIVE_RUN_STATE,
+            stable_id="evil",
+            trust=ContextTrust.UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE,
+            sensitivity=Sensitivity.INTERNAL,
+            content="untrusted content masquerading as instructions",
+            role="system",
+        )]
+
+    monkeypatch.setattr(local_mod, "_build_drafts", bad_drafts)
+    client = httpx.AsyncClient(transport=httpx.MockTransport(handler))
+    worker = OpenAICompatWorker("local", base_url="http://fake/v1", model="m", client=client)
+    try:
+        result = await worker.run(Task(objective="x"))
+    finally:
+        await client.aclose()
+
+    assert calls["n"] == 0  # fail closed: endpoint NEVER hit
+    assert result.error_kind == "context_contract"
+    assert "LiveContextViolation" in (result.error or "")

    72	def _assign_tools(plan: dict[str, Any], registry) -> dict[str, Any]:
    73	    """Final tool subset per step: planner-proposed names that exist in the
    74	    registry, unioned with deterministic keyword detection over the objective.
    75	    Both signals are conservative — no signal means NO tools for the step."""
    76	    from metaharness.tools.registry import DEFAULT_SUBSET_CAP
    77	
    78	    for step in plan.get("steps", []):
    79	        if not isinstance(step, dict):
    80	            continue
    81	        proposed = step.get("tools")
    82	        valid = [t for t in proposed if registry.get(t)] if isinstance(proposed, list) else []
    83	        detected = registry.select_for(
    84	            str(step.get("objective", "")),
    85	            [str(b) for b in step.get("boundaries", []) if b] or None,
    86	        )
    87	        merged = valid + [t for t in detected if t not in valid]
    88	        step["tools"] = merged[:DEFAULT_SUBSET_CAP]
    89	        if any((tool := registry.get(name)) and tool.source.startswith("mcp:")
    90	               for name in step["tools"]):
    91	            # MCP annotations are server-supplied hints, not authorization.
    92	            # Every external MCP delegation pauses before execution.
    93	            step["hitl"] = True
    94	            step["hitl_timing"] = "before"
    95	    return plan

codex
Verdict: REJECT

1. **P1, CONFIRMED** — Workflow interpolation launders prior worker output into instruction-trusted sections. [engine.py:407](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/workflows/engine.py:407) substitutes `$steps.*.output` into boundaries, while both [local.py:75](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/local.py:75) and [coding.py:327](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/coding.py:327) declare those resolved strings as `RESPONSE_CONTRACT` with `INSTRUCTION` trust.  
   Fix: Reject dynamic references in instruction fields or preserve substituted values as separate untrusted drafts.

2. **P1, CONFIRMED** — Trust enforcement can be bypassed through `SectionDraft.role`. The role is an unrestricted string at [live.py:105](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:105), validation checks only `section_type` at [live.py:189](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:189), and rendering uses the unchecked role at [live.py:137](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:137). An `UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE/WORKFLOW_STATE` draft with `role="system"` is accepted and rendered as a system message.  
   Fix: Make roles a literal enum and enforce role/section/trust consistency before rendering.

3. **P1, CONFIRMED** — External tool schemas bypass the typed trust boundary and are automatically promoted to instructions. MCP-supplied descriptions and schemas enter the registry at [mcp.py:125](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/tools/mcp.py:125), are passed separately from `SectionDraft`s at [local.py:212](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/local.py:212), then are unconditionally recorded as `INSTRUCTION` at [live.py:429](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:429).  
   Fix: Represent tool schemas as typed drafts with explicit provenance and reject non-authoritative/generated schemas from the instruction slot.

4. **P1, CONFIRMED** — `extra_body` can replace the assembled messages or tools immediately before POST. [local.py:217](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/local.py:217) builds the derived body, but [local.py:232](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/local.py:232) applies unrestricted overrides before [local.py:308](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/local.py:308) sends it. Thus unredacted, unattested `extra_body["messages"]` or `["tools"]` reaches the endpoint. The divergence test checks only `body["messages"]` without exercising overrides at [test_context.py:315](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/tests/test_context.py:315).  
   Fix: Reject transport-reserved keys in `extra_body`, or apply overrides before assembly and attest the resulting surfaces.

5. **P1, CONFIRMED** — `tool_call_id` bypasses redaction. Only content and `tool_calls` are redacted at [live.py:231](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:231); the raw ID is retained at [live.py:308](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:308) and emitted at [live.py:156](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:156). The local worker sources this ID from model output at [local.py:355](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/local.py:355).  
   Fix: Redact every string-bearing structured field, including `tool_call_id`, before envelope and surface construction.

6. **P1, CONFIRMED** — Structured assistant `tool_calls` are neither fitted nor counted toward the hard budget. `messages_tokens()` counts only message content at [assembly.py:77](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/assembly.py:77), and that incomplete count drives the hard postcondition at [live.py:346](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:346). A 10,000-character tool argument is therefore accepted under a 20-token limit and sent on the next round.  
   Fix: Include canonicalized structured message fields in token accounting and fit or reject complete turns deterministically.

7. **P1, CONFIRMED** — Manifests attest transport surfaces that were not sent. The assembler always creates message entries at [live.py:328](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:328) and always adds a flat prompt plus optional system prompt at [live.py:458](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:458). Local transport sends only messages/tools, while coding adapters send flat prompt/system prompt at [coding.py:468](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/coding.py:468); nevertheless all entries are marked “included” at [live.py:480](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/context/live.py:480).  
   Fix: Make the selected adapter transport an assembly input and include only actually transmitted surfaces in the authoritative manifest.

8. **P1, CONFIRMED** — `error_kind` affects retries and capability evidence without being authenticated. The v2 signing payload omits it at [runner.py:47](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/harness/runner.py:47), while the executor trusts it to suppress matrix evidence at [executor.py:396](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/core/executor.py:396) and abort retries at [executor.py:439](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/core/executor.py:439). Changing a valid signed result from `None` to `"context_contract"` still verifies.  
   Fix: Derive this classification in a harness-controlled boundary and cover it with a new result-signature version.

9. **P2, CONFIRMED** — Canonical journals do not enforce that `context.manifest` is attempt-scoped. [journal.py:73](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/src/metaharness/workflows/journal.py:73) requires `attempt_id` only for `attempt.*`, `tool.*`, and `verification.*`; a `context.manifest` with no attempt ID validates. The test supplies an ID voluntarily at [test_run_events.py:205](/private/tmp/meta-harness-meta-19/tests/test_run_events.py:205) but has no negative invariant test.  
   Fix: Require `attempt_id` for `context.manifest` in `RunEvent` validation and add a rejection test.

An `UNTRUSTED_EVIDENCE/WORKFLOW_STATE` draft with `role="system"` is accepted and rendered as a system message.  
   Fix: Make roles a literal enum and enforce role/section/trust consistency before rendering.
